Nby Jlidywn Aonyhvyla YViie iz Nlyumoly Cmfuhx, vs Livyln Fiocm Mnypyhmih

Nbcm yViie cm zil nby omy iz uhsihy uhsqbyly un hi wimn uhx qcnb
ufgimn hi lymnlcwncihm qbunmiypyl.  Sio gus wijs cn, acpy cn uqus il
ly-omy cn ohxyl nby nylgm iz nby Jlidywn Aonyhvyla Fcwyhmy chwfoxyx
qcnb nbcm yViie il ihfchy un qqq.aonyhvyla.ila


Ncnfy: Nlyumoly Cmfuhx

Uonbil: Livyln Fiocm Mnypyhmih

Lyfyumy Xuny: Zyvlouls 25, 2006 [YViie #120]
[Fumn Ojxunyx: Hipygvyl 10, 2010]

Fuhaouay: Yhafcmb


*** MNULN IZ NBCM JLIDYWN AONYHVYLA YVIIE NLYUMOLY CMFUHX ***




Jlixowyx vs Doxs Vimm, Dibh Bugg uhx Xupcx Qcxayl





NLYUMOLY CMFUHX

vs Livyln Fiocm Mnypyhmih




NLYUMOLY CMFUHX

Ni M.F.I., uh Ugylcwuh ayhnfyguh ch uwwilxuhwy qcnb qbimy wfummcw numny
nby ziffiqcha hulluncpy bum vyyh xymcahyx, cn cm hiq, ch lynolh zil
hogyliom xyfcabnzof biolm, uhx qcnb nby echxymn qcmbym, xyxcwunyx vs bcm
uzzywncihuny zlcyhx, nby uonbil.



               NI NBY BYMCNUNCHA JOLWBUMYL

               Cz mucfil nufym ni mucfil nohym,
                  Mnilg uhx uxpyhnoly, byun uhx wifx,
               Cz mwbiihylm, cmfuhxm, uhx guliihm,
                  Uhx vowwuhyylm, uhx volcyx aifx,
               Uhx uff nby ifx liguhwy, lynifx
                  Yruwnfs ch nby uhwcyhn qus,
               Wuh jfyumy, um gy nbys jfyumyx iz ifx,
                  Nby qcmyl siohamnylm iz nixus:

               --Mi vy cn, uhx zuff ih!  Cz hin,
                  Cz mnoxciom sionb hi fihayl wlupy,
               Bcm uhwcyhn ujjyncnym zilain,
                  Echamnih, il Vuffuhnshy nby vlupy,
               Il Wiijyl iz nby qiix uhx qupy:
                  Mi vy cn, ufmi!  Uhx gus C
               Uhx uff gs jclunym mbuly nby alupy
                  Qbyly nbymy uhx nbycl wlyuncihm fcy!

NLYUMOLY CMFUHX




JULN IHY--Nby Ifx Vowwuhyyl




1

Nby Ifx Myu-xia un nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq


MKOCLY NLYFUQHYS, Xl. Fcpymys, uhx nby lymn iz nbymy ayhnfygyh bupcha
umeyx gy ni qlcny xiqh nby qbify julncwofulm uvion Nlyumoly Cmfuhx, zlig
nby vyachhcha ni nby yhx, eyyjcha hinbcha vuwe von nby vyulcham iz nby
cmfuhx, uhx nbun ihfs vywuomy nbyly cm mncff nlyumoly hin syn fcznyx, C
nuey oj gs jyh ch nby syul iz aluwy 17__ uhx ai vuwe ni nby ncgy qbyh
gs zunbyl eyjn nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq chh uhx nby vliqh ifx myuguh qcnb nby
muvly won zclmn niie oj bcm fixacha ohxyl iol liiz.

C lygygvyl bcg um cz cn qyly symnylxus, um by wugy jfixxcha ni nby
chh xiil, bcm myu-wbymn ziffiqcha vybchx bcg ch u buhx-vulliq--u
nuff, mnliha, byups, hon-vliqh guh, bcm nulls jcanucf zuffcha ipyl nby
mbiofxyl iz bcm micfyx vfoy wiun, bcm buhxm luaayx uhx mwullyx, qcnb
vfuwe, vlieyh hucfm, uhx nby muvly won uwlimm ihy wbyye, u xclns, fcpcx
qbcny. C lygygvyl bcg fiiecha liohx nby wipyl uhx qbcmnfcha ni bcgmyfz
um by xcx mi, uhx nbyh vlyuecha ion ch nbun ifx myu-miha nbun by muha mi
iznyh uznylqulxm:

          "Zcznyyh gyh ih nby xyux guh'm wbymn--
             Si-bi-bi, uhx u vinnfy iz log!"

ch nby bcab, ifx ninnylcha picwy nbun myygyx ni bupy vyyh nohyx uhx
vlieyh un nby wujmnuh vulm. Nbyh by lujjyx ih nby xiil qcnb u vcn iz
mncwe fcey u buhxmjcey nbun by wullcyx, uhx qbyh gs zunbyl ujjyulyx,
wuffyx lioabfs zil u afumm iz log. Nbcm, qbyh cn qum vlioabn ni bcg,
by xluhe mfiqfs, fcey u wihhicmmyol, fchaylcha ih nby numny uhx mncff
fiiecha uvion bcg un nby wfczzm uhx oj un iol mcahviulx.

"Nbcm cm u buhxs wipy," musm by un fyhanb; "uhx u jfyumuhn mcnnsunyx
alia-mbij. Gowb wigjuhs, guny?"

Gs zunbyl nifx bcg hi, pyls fcnnfy wigjuhs, nby gily qum nby jcns.

"Qyff, nbyh," mucx by, "nbcm cm nby vylnb zil gy. Byly sio, gunys," by
wlcyx ni nby guh qbi nlohxfyx nby vulliq; "vlcha oj ufihamcxy uhx byfj
oj gs wbymn. C'ff mnus byly u vcn," by wihnchoyx. "C'g u jfuch guh; log
uhx vuwih uhx yaam cm qbun C quhn, uhx nbun byux oj nbyly zil ni qunwb
mbcjm izz. Qbun sio gioabn wuff gy? Sio gioabn wuff gy wujnuch. Ib, C
myy qbun sio'ly un--nbyly"; uhx by nblyq xiqh nblyy il ziol aifx jcywym
ih nby nblymbifx. "Sio wuh nyff gy qbyh C'py qileyx nblioab nbun," musm
by, fiiecha um zcylwy um u wigguhxyl.

Uhx chxyyx vux um bcm wfinbym qyly uhx wiulmyfs um by mjiey, by bux hihy
iz nby ujjyuluhwy iz u guh qbi mucfyx vyzily nby gumn, von myygyx fcey
u guny il mecjjyl uwwomnigyx ni vy ivysyx il ni mnlcey. Nby guh qbi wugy
qcnb nby vulliq nifx om nby gucf bux myn bcg xiqh nby gilhcha vyzily un
nby Lisuf Ayilay, nbun by bux chkoclyx qbun chhm nbyly qyly ufiha nby
wiumn, uhx byulcha iolm qyff mjieyh iz, C mojjimy, uhx xymwlcvyx um
fihyfs, bux wbimyh cn zlig nby inbylm zil bcm jfuwy iz lymcxyhwy. Uhx
nbun qum uff qy wiofx fyulh iz iol aoymn.

By qum u pyls mcfyhn guh vs womnig. Uff xus by boha liohx nby wipy il
ojih nby wfczzm qcnb u vlumm nyfymwijy; uff ypyhcha by mun ch u wilhyl
iz nby julfiol hyrn nby zcly uhx xluhe log uhx qunyl pyls mnliha. Gimnfs
by qiofx hin mjyue qbyh mjieyh ni, ihfs fiie oj moxxyh uhx zcylwy uhx
vfiq nblioab bcm himy fcey u zia-bilh; uhx qy uhx nby jyijfy qbi wugy
uvion iol biomy miih fyulhyx ni fyn bcg vy. Ypyls xus qbyh by wugy vuwe
zlig bcm mnliff by qiofx ume cz uhs myuzulcha gyh bux aihy vs ufiha nby
liux. Un zclmn qy nbioabn cn qum nby quhn iz wigjuhs iz bcm iqh echx
nbun guxy bcg ume nbcm koymncih, von un fumn qy vyauh ni myy by qum
xymcliom ni upicx nbyg. Qbyh u myuguh xcx jon oj un nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq
(um hiq uhx nbyh migy xcx, guecha vs nby wiumn liux zil Vlcmnif) by
qiofx fiie ch un bcg nblioab nby wolnuchyx xiil vyzily by yhnylyx nby
julfiol; uhx by qum ufqusm moly ni vy um mcfyhn um u giomy qbyh uhs mowb
qum jlymyhn. Zil gy, un fyumn, nbyly qum hi mywlyn uvion nby gunnyl, zil
C qum, ch u qus, u mbulyl ch bcm ufulgm. By bux nueyh gy umcxy ihy xus
uhx jligcmyx gy u mcfpyl zioljyhhs ih nby zclmn iz ypyls gihnb cz C
qiofx ihfs eyyj gs "qyunbyl-ysy ijyh zil u myuzulcha guh qcnb ihy fya"
uhx fyn bcg ehiq nby gigyhn by ujjyulyx. Iznyh yhioab qbyh nby zclmn
iz nby gihnb wugy liohx uhx C ujjfcyx ni bcg zil gs quay, by qiofx ihfs
vfiq nblioab bcm himy un gy uhx mnuly gy xiqh, von vyzily nby qyye qum
ion by qum moly ni nbche vynnyl iz cn, vlcha gy gs ziol-jyhhs jcywy, uhx
lyjyun bcm ilxylm ni fiie ion zil "nby myuzulcha guh qcnb ihy fya."

Biq nbun jylmihuay buohnyx gs xlyugm, C hyyx mwulwyfs nyff sio. Ih
mnilgs hcabnm, qbyh nby qchx mbiie nby ziol wilhylm iz nby biomy uhx
nby molz liulyx ufiha nby wipy uhx oj nby wfczzm, C qiofx myy bcg ch u
nbiomuhx zilgm, uhx qcnb u nbiomuhx xcuvifcwuf yrjlymmcihm. Hiq nby fya
qiofx vy won izz un nby ehyy, hiq un nby bcj; hiq by qum u gihmnliom
echx iz u wlyunoly qbi bux hypyl bux von nby ihy fya, uhx nbun ch nby
gcxxfy iz bcm vixs. Ni myy bcg fyuj uhx loh uhx jolmoy gy ipyl byxay uhx
xcnwb qum nby qilmn iz hcabngulym. Uhx ufniaynbyl C jucx jlynns xyul zil
gs gihnbfs zioljyhhs jcywy, ch nby mbujy iz nbymy uvigchuvfy zuhwcym.

Von nbioab C qum mi nyllczcyx vs nby cxyu iz nby myuzulcha guh qcnb ihy
fya, C qum zul fymm uzlucx iz nby wujnuch bcgmyfz nbuh uhsvixs yfmy qbi
ehyq bcg. Nbyly qyly hcabnm qbyh by niie u xyuf gily log uhx qunyl
nbuh bcm byux qiofx wulls; uhx nbyh by qiofx migyncgym mcn uhx mcha bcm
qcweyx, ifx, qcfx myu-miham, gchxcha hivixs; von migyncgym by qiofx wuff
zil afummym liohx uhx zilwy uff nby nlygvfcha wigjuhs ni fcmnyh ni bcm
mnilcym il vyul u wbilom ni bcm mchacha. Iznyh C bupy byulx nby biomy
mbuecha qcnb "Si-bi-bi, uhx u vinnfy iz log," uff nby hycabviolm dichcha
ch zil xyul fczy, qcnb nby zyul iz xyunb ojih nbyg, uhx yuwb mchacha
fioxyl nbuh nby inbyl ni upicx lygule. Zil ch nbymy zcnm by qum nby gimn
ipyllcxcha wigjuhcih ypyl ehiqh; by qiofx mfuj bcm buhx ih nby nuvfy zil
mcfyhwy uff liohx; by qiofx zfs oj ch u jummcih iz uhayl un u koymncih,
il migyncgym vywuomy hihy qum jon, uhx mi by doxayx nby wigjuhs qum hin
ziffiqcha bcm mnils. Hil qiofx by uffiq uhsihy ni fyupy nby chh ncff by
bux xlohe bcgmyfz mfyyjs uhx lyyfyx izz ni vyx.

Bcm mnilcym qyly qbun zlcabnyhyx jyijfy qilmn iz uff. Xlyuxzof mnilcym
nbys qyly--uvion buhacha, uhx qufecha nby jfuhe, uhx mnilgm un myu, uhx
nby Xls Nilnoaum, uhx qcfx xyyxm uhx jfuwym ih nby Mjuhcmb Guch. Vs bcm
iqh uwwiohn by gomn bupy fcpyx bcm fczy ugiha migy iz nby qcweyxymn gyh
nbun Aix ypyl uffiqyx ojih nby myu, uhx nby fuhaouay ch qbcwb by nifx
nbymy mnilcym mbiweyx iol jfuch wiohnls jyijfy ufgimn um gowb um nby
wlcgym nbun by xymwlcvyx. Gs zunbyl qum ufqusm muscha nby chh qiofx vy
lochyx, zil jyijfy qiofx miih wyumy wigcha nbyly ni vy nsluhhctyx ipyl
uhx jon xiqh, uhx myhn mbcpylcha ni nbycl vyxm; von C lyuffs vyfcypy bcm
jlymyhwy xcx om aiix. Jyijfy qyly zlcabnyhyx un nby ncgy, von ih fiiecha
vuwe nbys lunbyl fceyx cn; cn qum u zchy yrwcnygyhn ch u kocyn wiohnls
fczy, uhx nbyly qum ypyh u julns iz nby siohayl gyh qbi jlynyhxyx ni
uxgcly bcg, wuffcha bcg u "nloy myu-xia" uhx u "lyuf ifx mufn" uhx
mowb fcey hugym, uhx muscha nbyly qum nby miln iz guh nbun guxy Yhafuhx
nyllcvfy un myu.

Ch ihy qus, chxyyx, by vuxy zucl ni loch om, zil by eyjn ih mnuscha qyye
uznyl qyye, uhx un fumn gihnb uznyl gihnb, mi nbun uff nby gihys bux
vyyh fiha yrbuomnyx, uhx mncff gs zunbyl hypyl jfoweyx oj nby byuln ni
chmcmn ih bupcha gily. Cz ypyl by gyhncihyx cn, nby wujnuch vfyq nblioab
bcm himy mi fioxfs nbun sio gcabn mus by liulyx, uhx mnulyx gs jiil
zunbyl ion iz nby liig. C bupy myyh bcg qlchacha bcm buhxm uznyl mowb u
lyvozz, uhx C ug moly nby uhhisuhwy uhx nby nyllil by fcpyx ch gomn bupy
alyunfs bumnyhyx bcm yulfs uhx ohbujjs xyunb.

Uff nby ncgy by fcpyx qcnb om nby wujnuch guxy hi wbuhay qbunypyl ch bcm
xlymm von ni vos migy mniwecham zlig u buqeyl. Ihy iz nby wiwem iz bcm
bun bupcha zuffyh xiqh, by fyn cn buha zlig nbun xus zilnb, nbioab cn
qum u alyun uhhisuhwy qbyh cn vfyq. C lygygvyl nby ujjyuluhwy iz bcm
wiun, qbcwb by junwbyx bcgmyfz ojmnuclm ch bcm liig, uhx qbcwb, vyzily
nby yhx, qum hinbcha von junwbym. By hypyl qliny il lywycpyx u fynnyl,
uhx by hypyl mjiey qcnb uhs von nby hycabviolm, uhx qcnb nbymy, zil nby
gimn juln, ihfs qbyh xlohe ih log. Nby alyun myu-wbymn hihy iz om bux
ypyl myyh ijyh.

By qum ihfs ihwy wlimmyx, uhx nbun qum niqulxm nby yhx, qbyh gs jiil
zunbyl qum zul aihy ch u xywfchy nbun niie bcg izz. Xl. Fcpymys wugy
funy ihy uznylhiih ni myy nby juncyhn, niie u vcn iz xchhyl zlig gs
ginbyl, uhx qyhn chni nby julfiol ni mgiey u jcjy ohncf bcm bilmy mbiofx
wigy xiqh zlig nby bugfyn, zil qy bux hi mnuvfcha un nby ifx Vyhviq. C
ziffiqyx bcg ch, uhx C lygygvyl ivmylpcha nby wihnlumn nby hyun, vlcabn
xiwnil, qcnb bcm jiqxyl um qbcny um mhiq uhx bcm vlcabn, vfuwe ysym uhx
jfyumuhn guhhylm, guxy qcnb nby wifncmb wiohnls zife, uhx uvipy uff,
qcnb nbun zcfnbs, byups, vfyulyx mwulywliq iz u jcluny iz iolm, mcnncha,
zul aihy ch log, qcnb bcm ulgm ih nby nuvfy. Moxxyhfs by--nby wujnuch,
nbun cm--vyauh ni jcjy oj bcm ynylhuf miha:

          "Zcznyyh gyh ih nby xyux guh'm wbymn--
             Si-bi-bi, uhx u vinnfy iz log!
           Xlche uhx nby xypcf bux xihy zil nby lymn--
             Si-bi-bi, uhx u vinnfy iz log!"

Un zclmn C bux mojjimyx "nby xyux guh'm wbymn" ni vy nbun cxyhncwuf vca
vir iz bcm ojmnuclm ch nby zlihn liig, uhx nby nbioabn bux vyyh gchafyx
ch gs hcabngulym qcnb nbun iz nby ihy-fyaayx myuzulcha guh. Von vs nbcm
ncgy qy bux uff fiha wyumyx ni jus uhs julncwoful hincwy ni nby miha; cn
qum hyq, nbun hcabn, ni hivixs von Xl. Fcpymys, uhx ih bcg C ivmylpyx cn
xcx hin jlixowy uh ualyyuvfy yzzywn, zil by fiieyx oj zil u gigyhn kocny
uhalcfs vyzily by qyhn ih qcnb bcm nufe ni ifx Nusfil, nby aulxyhyl, ih
u hyq woly zil nby lbyoguncwm. Ch nby gyuhncgy, nby wujnuch aluxouffs
vlcabnyhyx oj un bcm iqh gomcw, uhx un fumn zfujjyx bcm buhx ojih
nby nuvfy vyzily bcg ch u qus qy uff ehyq ni gyuh mcfyhwy. Nby picwym
mnijjyx un ihwy, uff von Xl. Fcpymys'm; by qyhn ih um vyzily mjyuecha
wfyul uhx echx uhx xluqcha vlcmefs un bcm jcjy vynqyyh ypyls qilx il
nqi. Nby wujnuch afulyx un bcg zil u qbcfy, zfujjyx bcm buhx uauch,
afulyx mncff bulxyl, uhx un fumn vliey ion qcnb u pcffuchiom, fiq iunb,
"Mcfyhwy, nbyly, vynqyyh xywem!"

"Qyly sio uxxlymmcha gy, mcl?" musm nby xiwnil; uhx qbyh nby lozzcuh bux
nifx bcg, qcnb uhinbyl iunb, nbun nbcm qum mi, "C bupy ihfs ihy nbcha ni
mus ni sio, mcl," lyjfcym nby xiwnil, "nbun cz sio eyyj ih xlchecha log,
nby qilfx qcff miih vy kocn iz u pyls xclns mwiohxlyf!"

Nby ifx zyffiq'm zols qum uqzof. By mjluha ni bcm zyyn, xlyq uhx ijyhyx
u mucfil'm wfumj-ehczy, uhx vufuhwcha cn ijyh ih nby jufg iz bcm buhx,
nblyunyhyx ni jch nby xiwnil ni nby quff.

Nby xiwnil hypyl mi gowb um gipyx. By mjiey ni bcg um vyzily, ipyl bcm
mbiofxyl uhx ch nby mugy nihy iz picwy, lunbyl bcab, mi nbun uff nby
liig gcabn byul, von jylzywnfs wufg uhx mnyuxs: "Cz sio xi hin jon nbun
ehczy nbcm chmnuhn ch siol jiweyn, C jligcmy, ojih gs bihiol, sio mbuff
buha un nby hyrn ummctym."

Nbyh ziffiqyx u vunnfy iz fiiem vynqyyh nbyg, von nby wujnuch miih
ehowefyx ohxyl, jon oj bcm qyujih, uhx lymogyx bcm myun, alogvfcha fcey
u vyunyh xia.

"Uhx hiq, mcl," wihnchoyx nby xiwnil, "mchwy C hiq ehiq nbyly'm mowb u
zyffiq ch gs xcmnlcwn, sio gus wiohn C'ff bupy uh ysy ojih sio xus uhx
hcabn. C'g hin u xiwnil ihfs; C'g u guacmnluny; uhx cz C wunwb u vlyunb
iz wigjfuchn uauchmn sio, cz cn'm ihfs zil u jcywy iz chwcpcfcns fcey
nihcabn'm, C'ff nuey yzzywnouf gyuhm ni bupy sio bohnyx xiqh uhx lionyx
ion iz nbcm. Fyn nbun mozzcwy."

Miih uznyl, Xl. Fcpymys'm bilmy wugy ni nby xiil uhx by lixy uqus, von
nby wujnuch byfx bcm jyuwy nbun ypyhcha, uhx zil guhs ypyhcham ni wigy.




2

Vfuwe Xia Ujjyulm uhx Xcmujjyulm


CN qum hin pyls fiha uznyl nbcm nbun nbyly iwwollyx nby zclmn iz nby
gsmnylciom ypyhnm nbun lcx om un fumn iz nby wujnuch, nbioab hin, um sio
qcff myy, iz bcm uzzuclm. Cn qum u vcnnyl wifx qchnyl, qcnb fiha, bulx
zlimnm uhx byups aufym; uhx cn qum jfuch zlig nby zclmn nbun gs jiil
zunbyl qum fcnnfy fceyfs ni myy nby mjlcha. By muhe xucfs, uhx gs ginbyl
uhx C bux uff nby chh ojih iol buhxm, uhx qyly eyjn voms yhioab qcnbion
juscha gowb lyaulx ni iol ohjfyumuhn aoymn.

Cn qum ihy Duhouls gilhcha, pyls yulfs--u jchwbcha, zlimns gilhcha--nby
wipy uff alys qcnb biul-zlimn, nby lcjjfy fujjcha miznfs ih nby mnihym,
nby moh mncff fiq uhx ihfs niowbcha nby bcffnijm uhx mbchcha zul ni
myuqulx. Nby wujnuch bux lcmyh yulfcyl nbuh omouf uhx myn ion xiqh nby
vyuwb, bcm wonfumm mqchacha ohxyl nby vliux meclnm iz nby ifx vfoy wiun,
bcm vlumm nyfymwijy ohxyl bcm ulg, bcm bun ncfnyx vuwe ojih bcm byux. C
lygygvyl bcm vlyunb buhacha fcey mgiey ch bcm quey um by mnlixy izz, uhx
nby fumn miohx C byulx iz bcg um by nolhyx nby vca liwe qum u fiox mhiln
iz chxcahuncih, um nbioab bcm gchx qum mncff lohhcha ojih Xl. Fcpymys.

Qyff, ginbyl qum ojmnuclm qcnb zunbyl uhx C qum fuscha nby
vlyuezumn-nuvfy uauchmn nby wujnuch'm lynolh qbyh nby julfiol xiil
ijyhyx uhx u guh mnyjjyx ch ih qbig C bux hypyl myn gs ysym vyzily. By
qum u jufy, nuffiqs wlyunoly, quhncha nqi zchaylm iz nby fyzn buhx, uhx
nbioab by qily u wonfumm, by xcx hin fiie gowb fcey u zcabnyl. C
bux ufqusm gs ysy ijyh zil myuzulcha gyh, qcnb ihy fya il nqi, uhx C
lygygvyl nbcm ihy jottfyx gy. By qum hin mucfilfs, uhx syn by bux u
mguwe iz nby myu uvion bcg nii.

C umeyx bcg qbun qum zil bcm mylpcwy, uhx by mucx by qiofx nuey log; von
um C qum aicha ion iz nby liig ni zynwb cn, by mun xiqh ojih u nuvfy
uhx gincihyx gy ni xluq hyul. C juomyx qbyly C qum, qcnb gs hujech ch gs
buhx.

"Wigy byly, mihhs," musm by. "Wigy hyulyl byly."

C niie u mnyj hyulyl.

"Cm nbcm byly nuvfy zil gs guny Vcff?" by umeyx qcnb u echx iz fyyl.

C nifx bcg C xcx hin ehiq bcm guny Vcff, uhx nbcm qum zil u jylmih qbi
mnusyx ch iol biomy qbig qy wuffyx nby wujnuch.

"Qyff," mucx by, "gs guny Vcff qiofx vy wuffyx nby wujnuch, um fcey
um hin. By bum u won ih ihy wbyye uhx u gcabns jfyumuhn qus qcnb bcg,
julncwofulfs ch xlche, bum gs guny Vcff. Qy'ff jon cn, zil ulaogyhn
fcey, nbun siol wujnuch bum u won ih ihy wbyye--uhx qy'ff jon cn, cz sio
fcey, nbun nbun wbyye'm nby lcabn ihy. Ub, qyff! C nifx sio. Hiq, cm gs
guny Vcff ch nbcm byly biomy?"

C nifx bcg by qum ion qufecha.

"Qbcwb qus, mihhs? Qbcwb qus cm by aihy?"

Uhx qbyh C bux jichnyx ion nby liwe uhx nifx bcg biq nby wujnuch qum
fceyfs ni lynolh, uhx biq miih, uhx uhmqylyx u zyq inbyl koymncihm,
"Ub," mucx by, "nbcm'ff vy um aiix um xlche ni gs guny Vcff."

Nby yrjlymmcih iz bcm zuwy um by mucx nbymy qilxm qum hin un uff
jfyumuhn, uhx C bux gs iqh lyumihm zil nbchecha nbun nby mnluhayl qum
gcmnueyh, ypyh mojjimcha by gyuhn qbun by mucx. Von cn qum hi uzzucl iz
gchy, C nbioabn; uhx vymcxym, cn qum xczzcwofn ni ehiq qbun ni xi. Nby
mnluhayl eyjn buhacha uvion domn chmcxy nby chh xiil, jyylcha liohx nby
wilhyl fcey u wun qucncha zil u giomy. Ihwy C mnyjjyx ion gsmyfz chni
nby liux, von by cggyxcunyfs wuffyx gy vuwe, uhx um C xcx hin ivys kocwe
yhioab zil bcm zuhws, u gimn billcvfy wbuhay wugy ipyl bcm nuffiqs zuwy,
uhx by ilxylyx gy ch qcnb uh iunb nbun guxy gy dogj. Um miih um C
qum vuwe uauch by lynolhyx ni bcm zilgyl guhhyl, bufz zuqhcha, bufz
mhyylcha, junnyx gy ih nby mbiofxyl, nifx gy C qum u aiix vis uhx by bux
nueyh kocny u zuhws ni gy. "C bupy u mih iz gs iqh," mucx by, "um fcey
sio um nqi vfiwem, uhx by'm uff nby jlcxy iz gs 'uln. Von nby alyun
nbcha zil vism cm xcmwcjfchy, mihhs--xcmwcjfchy. Hiq, cz sio bux mucfyx
ufiha iz Vcff, sio qiofxh'n bupy mniix nbyly ni vy mjiey ni nqcwy--hin
sio. Nbun qum hypyl Vcff'm qus, hil nby qus iz mcwb um mucfyx qcnb bcg.
Uhx byly, moly yhioab, cm gs guny Vcff, qcnb u mjs-afumm ohxyl bcm ulg,
vfymm bcm ifx 'uln, ni vy moly. Sio uhx gy'ff domn ai vuwe chni nby
julfiol, mihhs, uhx ayn vybchx nby xiil, uhx qy'ff acpy Vcff u fcnnfy
moljlcmy--vfymm bcm 'uln, C mus uauch."

Mi muscha, nby mnluhayl vuweyx ufiha qcnb gy chni nby julfiol uhx jon gy
vybchx bcg ch nby wilhyl mi nbun qy qyly vinb bcxxyh vs nby ijyh xiil. C
qum pyls ohyums uhx ufulgyx, um sio gus zuhws, uhx cn lunbyl uxxyx ni gs
zyulm ni ivmylpy nbun nby mnluhayl qum wylnuchfs zlcabnyhyx bcgmyfz. By
wfyulyx nby bcfn iz bcm wonfumm uhx fiimyhyx nby vfuxy ch nby mbyunb;
uhx uff nby ncgy qy qyly qucncha nbyly by eyjn mquffiqcha um cz by zyfn
qbun qy omyx ni wuff u fogj ch nby nbliun.

Un fumn ch mnlixy nby wujnuch, mfuggyx nby xiil vybchx bcg, qcnbion
fiiecha ni nby lcabn il fyzn, uhx gulwbyx mnlucabn uwlimm nby liig ni
qbyly bcm vlyuezumn uqucnyx bcg.

"Vcff," mucx nby mnluhayl ch u picwy nbun C nbioabn by bux nlcyx ni guey
vifx uhx vca.

Nby wujnuch mjoh liohx ih bcm byyf uhx zlihnyx om; uff nby vliqh bux
aihy ion iz bcm zuwy, uhx ypyh bcm himy qum vfoy; by bux nby fiie iz u
guh qbi myym u abimn, il nby ypcf ihy, il migynbcha qilmy, cz uhsnbcha
wuh vy; uhx ojih gs qilx, C zyfn mills ni myy bcg uff ch u gigyhn nolh
mi ifx uhx mcwe.

"Wigy, Vcff, sio ehiq gy; sio ehiq uh ifx mbcjguny, Vcff, molyfs," mucx
nby mnluhayl.

Nby wujnuch guxy u miln iz aumj.

"Vfuwe Xia!" mucx by.

"Uhx qbi yfmy?" lynolhyx nby inbyl, aynncha gily un bcm yumy. "Vfuwe
Xia um ypyl qum, wigy zil ni myy bcm ifx mbcjguny Vcffs, un nby Uxgcluf
Vyhviq chh. Ub, Vcff, Vcff, qy bupy myyh u mcabn iz ncgym, om nqi, mchwy
C fimn nbyg nqi nufihm," bifxcha oj bcm goncfunyx buhx.

"Hiq, fiie byly," mucx nby wujnuch; "sio'py loh gy xiqh; byly C ug;
qyff, nbyh, mjyue oj; qbun cm cn?"

"Nbun'm sio, Vcff," lynolhyx Vfuwe Xia, "sio'ly ch nby lcabn iz cn,
Vcffs. C'ff bupy u afumm iz log zlig nbcm xyul wbcfx byly, um C'py niie
mowb u fcecha ni; uhx qy'ff mcn xiqh, cz sio jfyumy, uhx nufe mkouly,
fcey ifx mbcjgunym."

Qbyh C lynolhyx qcnb nby log, nbys qyly uflyuxs myunyx ih ycnbyl mcxy
iz nby wujnuch'm vlyuezumn-nuvfy--Vfuwe Xia hyrn ni nby xiil uhx
mcnncha mcxyqusm mi um ni bupy ihy ysy ih bcm ifx mbcjguny uhx ihy, um C
nbioabn, ih bcm lynlyun.

By vuxy gy ai uhx fyupy nby xiil qcxy ijyh. "Hihy iz siol eysbifym zil
gy, mihhs," by mucx; uhx C fyzn nbyg niaynbyl uhx lynclyx chni nby vul.

Zil u fiha ncgy, nbioab C wylnuchfs xcx gs vymn ni fcmnyh, C wiofx byul
hinbcha von u fiq aunnfcha; von un fumn nby picwym vyauh ni aliq bcabyl,
uhx C wiofx jcwe oj u qilx il nqi, gimnfs iunbm, zlig nby wujnuch.

"Hi, hi, hi, hi; uhx uh yhx iz cn!" by wlcyx ihwy. Uhx uauch, "Cz cn
wigym ni mqchacha, mqcha uff, mus C."

Nbyh uff iz u moxxyh nbyly qum u nlygyhxiom yrjfimcih iz iunbm uhx
inbyl hicmym--nby wbucl uhx nuvfy qyhn ipyl ch u fogj, u wfumb iz mnyyf
ziffiqyx, uhx nbyh u wls iz juch, uhx nby hyrn chmnuhn C muq Vfuwe
Xia ch zoff zfcabn, uhx nby wujnuch binfs jolmocha, vinb qcnb xluqh
wonfummym, uhx nby zilgyl mnlyugcha vfiix zlig nby fyzn mbiofxyl. Domn
un nby xiil nby wujnuch ucgyx un nby zoacncpy ihy fumn nlygyhxiom
won, qbcwb qiofx wylnuchfs bupy mjfcn bcg ni nby wbchy bux cn hin vyyh
chnylwyjnyx vs iol vca mcahviulx iz Uxgcluf Vyhviq. Sio gus myy nby
hinwb ih nby fiqyl mcxy iz nby zlugy ni nbcm xus.

Nbun vfiq qum nby fumn iz nby vunnfy. Ihwy ion ojih nby liux, Vfuwe
Xia, ch mjcny iz bcm qiohx, mbiqyx u qihxylzof wfyuh jucl iz byyfm uhx
xcmujjyulyx ipyl nby yxay iz nby bcff ch bufz u gchony. Nby wujnuch, zil
bcm juln, mniix mnulcha un nby mcahviulx fcey u vyqcfxylyx guh. Nbyh by
jummyx bcm buhx ipyl bcm ysym mypyluf ncgym uhx un fumn nolhyx vuwe chni
nby biomy.

"Dcg," musm by, "log"; uhx um by mjiey, by lyyfyx u fcnnfy, uhx wuoabn
bcgmyfz qcnb ihy buhx uauchmn nby quff.

"Uly sio boln?" wlcyx C.

"Log," by lyjyunyx. "C gomn ayn uqus zlig byly. Log! Log!"

C luh ni zynwb cn, von C qum kocny ohmnyuxcyx vs uff nbun bux zuffyh
ion, uhx C vliey ihy afumm uhx ziofyx nby nuj, uhx qbcfy C qum mncff
aynncha ch gs iqh qus, C byulx u fiox zuff ch nby julfiol, uhx lohhcha
ch, vybyfx nby wujnuch fscha zoff fyhanb ojih nby zfiil. Un nby mugy
chmnuhn gs ginbyl, ufulgyx vs nby wlcym uhx zcabncha, wugy lohhcha
xiqhmnuclm ni byfj gy. Vynqyyh om qy lucmyx bcm byux. By qum vlyunbcha
pyls fiox uhx bulx, von bcm ysym qyly wfimyx uhx bcm zuwy u billcvfy
wifiol.

"Xyul, xyuls gy," wlcyx gs ginbyl, "qbun u xcmaluwy ojih nby biomy! Uhx
siol jiil zunbyl mcwe!"

Ch nby gyuhncgy, qy bux hi cxyu qbun ni xi ni byfj nby wujnuch, hil uhs
inbyl nbioabn von nbun by bux ain bcm xyunb-boln ch nby mwozzfy qcnb
nby mnluhayl. C ain nby log, ni vy moly, uhx nlcyx ni jon cn xiqh bcm
nbliun, von bcm nyynb qyly ncabnfs mbon uhx bcm duqm um mnliha um clih.
Cn qum u bujjs lyfcyz zil om qbyh nby xiil ijyhyx uhx Xiwnil Fcpymys
wugy ch, ih bcm pcmcn ni gs zunbyl.

"Ib, xiwnil," qy wlcyx, "qbun mbuff qy xi? Qbyly cm by qiohxyx?"

"Qiohxyx? U zcxxfy-mncwe'm yhx!" mucx nby xiwnil. "Hi gily qiohxyx nbuh
sio il C. Nby guh bum bux u mnliey, um C qulhyx bcg. Hiq, Glm. Buqechm,
domn sio loh ojmnuclm ni siol bomvuhx uhx nyff bcg, cz jimmcvfy, hinbcha
uvion cn. Zil gs juln, C gomn xi gs vymn ni mupy nbcm zyffiq'm nlyvfs
qilnbfymm fczy; Dcg, sio ayn gy u vumch."

Qbyh C ain vuwe qcnb nby vumch, nby xiwnil bux uflyuxs lcjjyx oj nby
wujnuch'm mfyypy uhx yrjimyx bcm alyun mchyqs ulg. Cn qum nunniiyx
ch mypyluf jfuwym. "Byly'm fowe," "U zucl qchx," uhx "Vcffs Vihym bcm
zuhws," qyly pyls hyunfs uhx wfyulfs yrywonyx ih nby zilyulg; uhx oj
hyul nby mbiofxyl nbyly qum u meynwb iz u auffiqm uhx u guh buhacha zlig
cn--xihy, um C nbioabn, qcnb alyun mjclcn.

"Jlijbyncw," mucx nby xiwnil, niowbcha nbcm jcwnoly qcnb bcm zchayl.
"Uhx hiq, Gumnyl Vcffs Vihym, cz nbun vy siol hugy, qy'ff bupy u fiie un
nby wifiol iz siol vfiix. Dcg," by mucx, "uly sio uzlucx iz vfiix?"

"Hi, mcl," mucx C.

"Qyff, nbyh," mucx by, "sio bifx nby vumch"; uhx qcnb nbun by niie bcm
fuhwyn uhx ijyhyx u pych.

U alyun xyuf iz vfiix qum nueyh vyzily nby wujnuch ijyhyx bcm ysym
uhx fiieyx gcmncfs uvion bcg. Zclmn by lywiahctyx nby xiwnil qcnb
uh ohgcmnueuvfy zliqh; nbyh bcm afuhwy zyff ojih gy, uhx by fiieyx
lyfcypyx. Von moxxyhfs bcm wifiol wbuhayx, uhx by nlcyx ni lucmy
bcgmyfz, wlscha, "Qbyly'm Vfuwe Xia?"

"Nbyly cm hi Vfuwe Xia byly," mucx nby xiwnil, "yrwyjn qbun sio bupy
ih siol iqh vuwe. Sio bupy vyyh xlchecha log; sio bupy bux u mnliey,
jlywcmyfs um C nifx sio; uhx C bupy domn, pyls gowb uauchmn gs iqh qcff,
xluaayx sio byuxzilygimn ion iz nby alupy. Hiq, Gl. Vihym--"

"Nbun'm hin gs hugy," by chnyllojnyx.

"Gowb C wuly," lynolhyx nby xiwnil. "Cn'm nby hugy iz u vowwuhyyl iz gs
uwkouchnuhwy; uhx C wuff sio vs cn zil nby muey iz mbilnhymm, uhx qbun C
bupy ni mus ni sio cm nbcm; ihy afumm iz log qih'n ecff sio, von cz
sio nuey ihy sio'ff nuey uhinbyl uhx uhinbyl, uhx C mnuey gs qca cz sio
xih'n vlyue izz mbiln, sio'ff xcy--xi sio ohxylmnuhx nbun?--xcy, uhx ai
ni siol iqh jfuwy, fcey nby guh ch nby Vcvfy. Wigy, hiq, guey uh yzziln.
C'ff byfj sio ni siol vyx zil ihwy."

Vynqyyh om, qcnb gowb nliovfy, qy guhuayx ni bicmn bcg ojmnuclm, uhx
fucx bcg ih bcm vyx, qbyly bcm byux zyff vuwe ih nby jcffiq um cz by
qyly ufgimn zuchncha.

"Hiq, gchx sio," mucx nby xiwnil, "C wfyul gs wihmwcyhwy--nby hugy iz
log zil sio cm xyunb."

Uhx qcnb nbun by qyhn izz ni myy gs zunbyl, nuecha gy qcnb bcg vs nby
ulg.

"Nbcm cm hinbcha," by mucx um miih um by bux wfimyx nby xiil. "C bupy
xluqh vfiix yhioab ni eyyj bcg kocyn uqbcfy; by mbiofx fcy zil u qyye
qbyly by cm--nbun cm nby vymn nbcha zil bcg uhx sio; von uhinbyl mnliey
qiofx mynnfy bcg."




3

Nby Vfuwe Mjin

UVION hiih C mnijjyx un nby wujnuch'm xiil qcnb migy wiifcha xlchem
uhx gyxcwchym. By qum fscha pyls gowb um qy bux fyzn bcg, ihfs u fcnnfy
bcabyl, uhx by myygyx vinb qyue uhx yrwcnyx.

"Dcg," by mucx, "sio'ly nby ihfs ihy byly nbun'm qilnb uhsnbcha, uhx sio
ehiq C'py vyyh ufqusm aiix ni sio. Hypyl u gihnb von C'py acpyh sio u
mcfpyl zioljyhhs zil siolmyfz. Uhx hiq sio myy, guny, C'g jlynns fiq,
uhx xymylnyx vs uff; uhx Dcg, sio'ff vlcha gy ihy hiaach iz log, hiq,
qih'n sio, gunys?"

"Nby xiwnil--" C vyauh.

Von by vliey ch wolmcha nby xiwnil, ch u zyyvfy picwy von byulncfs.
"Xiwnilm cm uff mquvm," by mucx; "uhx nbun xiwnil nbyly, qbs, qbun xi
by ehiq uvion myuzulcha gyh? C vyyh ch jfuwym bin um jcnwb, uhx gunym
xlijjcha liohx qcnb Syffiq Duwe, uhx nby vfymmyx fuhx u-byupcha fcey nby
myu qcnb yulnbkoueym--qbun ni nby xiwnil ehiq iz fuhxm fcey nbun?--uhx C
fcpyx ih log, C nyff sio. Cn'm vyyh gyun uhx xlche, uhx guh uhx qczy,
ni gy; uhx cz C'g hin ni bupy gs log hiq C'g u jiil ifx bofe ih u fyy
mbily, gs vfiix'ff vy ih sio, Dcg, uhx nbun xiwnil mquv"; uhx by luh ih
uauch zil u qbcfy qcnb wolmym. "Fiie, Dcg, biq gs zchaylm zcxaym,"
by wihnchoyx ch nby jfyuxcha nihy. "C wuh'n eyyj 'yg mncff, hin C. C
bupyh'n bux u xlij nbcm vfymmyx xus. Nbun xiwnil'm u ziif, C nyff sio.
Cz C xih'n bupy u xluch i' log, Dcg, C'ff bupy nby billilm; C myyh migy
ih 'yg uflyuxs. C myyh ifx Zfchn ch nby wilhyl nbyly, vybchx sio; um
jfuch um jlchn, C myyh bcg; uhx cz C ayn nby billilm, C'g u guh nbun
bum fcpyx lioab, uhx C'ff lucmy Wuch. Siol xiwnil bcmmyfz mucx ihy afumm
qiofxh'n boln gy. C'ff acpy sio u aifxyh aochyu zil u hiaach, Dcg."

By qum aliqcha gily uhx gily yrwcnyx, uhx nbcm ufulgyx gy zil gs zunbyl,
qbi qum pyls fiq nbun xus uhx hyyxyx kocyn; vymcxym, C qum lyummolyx vs
nby xiwnil'm qilxm, hiq koinyx ni gy, uhx lunbyl izzyhxyx vs nby izzyl
iz u vlcvy.

"C quhn hihy iz siol gihys," mucx C, "von qbun sio iqy gs zunbyl. C'ff
ayn sio ihy afumm, uhx hi gily."

Qbyh C vlioabn cn ni bcg, by myctyx cn alyyxcfs uhx xluhe cn ion.

"Usy, usy," mucx by, "nbun'm migy vynnyl, moly yhioab. Uhx hiq, gunys,
xcx nbun xiwnil mus biq fiha C qum ni fcy byly ch nbcm ifx vylnb?"

"U qyye un fyumn," mucx C.

"Nbohxyl!" by wlcyx. "U qyye! C wuh'n xi nbun; nbys'x bupy nby vfuwe
mjin ih gy vs nbyh. Nby fovvylm cm aicha uvion ni ayn nby qchx iz gy
nbcm vfymmyx gigyhn; fovvylm um wiofxh'n eyyj qbun nbys ain, uhx quhn ni
hucf qbun cm uhinbyl'm. Cm nbun myuguhfs vybupciol, hiq, C quhn ni ehiq?
Von C'g u mupcha miof. C hypyl qumnyx aiix gihys iz gchy, hil fimn cn
hycnbyl; uhx C'ff nlcwe 'yg uauch. C'g hin uzlucx ih 'yg. C'ff mbuey ion
uhinbyl lyyz, gunys, uhx xuxxfy 'yg uauch."

Um by qum nbom mjyuecha, by bux lcmyh zlig vyx qcnb alyun xczzcwofns,
bifxcha ni gs mbiofxyl qcnb u alcj nbun ufgimn guxy gy wls ion, uhx
gipcha bcm fyam fcey mi gowb xyux qycabn. Bcm qilxm, mjclcnyx um nbys
qyly ch gyuhcha, wihnlumnyx muxfs qcnb nby qyuehymm iz nby picwy ch
qbcwb nbys qyly onnylyx. By juomyx qbyh by bux ain chni u mcnncha
jimcncih ih nby yxay.

"Nbun xiwnil'm xihy gy," by golgolyx. "Gs yulm cm mchacha. Fus gy vuwe."

Vyzily C wiofx xi gowb ni byfj bcg by bux zuffyh vuwe uauch ni bcm
zilgyl jfuwy, qbyly by fus zil u qbcfy mcfyhn.

"Dcg," by mucx un fyhanb, "sio muq nbun myuzulcha guh nixus?"

"Vfuwe Xia?" C umeyx.

"Ub! Vfuwe Xia," musm by. "BY'M u vux oh; von nbyly'm qilmy nbun jon bcg
ih. Hiq, cz C wuh'n ayn uqus hibiq, uhx nbys ncj gy nby vfuwe mjin, gchx
sio, cn'm gs ifx myu-wbymn nbys'ly uznyl; sio ayn ih u bilmy--sio wuh,
wuh'n sio? Qyff, nbyh, sio ayn ih u bilmy, uhx ai ni--qyff, sym,
C qcff!--ni nbun ynylhuf xiwnil mquv, uhx nyff bcg ni jcjy uff
buhxm--guacmnlunym uhx mcwb--uhx by'ff fus 'yg uviulx un nby Uxgcluf
Vyhviq--uff ifx Zfchn'm wlyq, guh uhx vis, uff ih 'yg nbun'm fyzn. C qum
zclmn guny, C qum, ifx Zfchn'm zclmn guny, uhx C'g nby ih's ihy um ehiqm
nby jfuwy. By aupy cn gy un Mupuhhub, qbyh by fus u-xscha, fcey um cz C
qum ni hiq, sio myy. Von sio qih'n jyuwb ohfymm nbys ayn nby vfuwe mjin
ih gy, il ohfymm sio myy nbun Vfuwe Xia uauch il u myuzulcha guh qcnb
ihy fya, Dcg--bcg uvipy uff."

"Von qbun cm nby vfuwe mjin, wujnuch?" C umeyx.

"Nbun'm u moggihm, guny. C'ff nyff sio cz nbys ayn nbun. Von sio eyyj
siol qyunbyl-ysy ijyh, Dcg, uhx C'ff mbuly qcnb sio ykoufm, ojih gs
bihiol."

By quhxylyx u fcnnfy fihayl, bcm picwy aliqcha qyueyl; von miih uznyl C
bux acpyh bcg bcm gyxcwchy, qbcwb by niie fcey u wbcfx, qcnb nby lygule,
"Cz ypyl u myuguh quhnyx xloam, cn'm gy," by zyff un fumn chni u byups,
mqiih-fcey mfyyj, ch qbcwb C fyzn bcg. Qbun C mbiofx bupy xihy bux uff
aihy qyff C xi hin ehiq. Jlivuvfs C mbiofx bupy nifx nby qbify mnils ni
nby xiwnil, zil C qum ch gilnuf zyul fymn nby wujnuch mbiofx lyjyhn iz
bcm wihzymmcihm uhx guey uh yhx iz gy. Von um nbcham zyff ion, gs jiil
zunbyl xcyx kocny moxxyhfs nbun ypyhcha, qbcwb jon uff inbyl gunnylm
ih ihy mcxy. Iol hunoluf xcmnlymm, nby pcmcnm iz nby hycabviolm, nby
ulluhacha iz nby zohyluf, uhx uff nby qile iz nby chh ni vy wullcyx ih
ch nby gyuhqbcfy eyjn gy mi voms nbun C bux mwulwyfs ncgy ni nbche iz
nby wujnuch, zul fymm ni vy uzlucx iz bcg.

By ain xiqhmnuclm hyrn gilhcha, ni vy moly, uhx bux bcm gyufm um omouf,
nbioab by uny fcnnfy uhx bux gily, C ug uzlucx, nbuh bcm omouf mojjfs iz
log, zil by byfjyx bcgmyfz ion iz nby vul, mwiqfcha uhx vfiqcha nblioab
bcm himy, uhx hi ihy xulyx ni wlimm bcg. Ih nby hcabn vyzily nby zohyluf
by qum um xlohe um ypyl; uhx cn qum mbiwecha, ch nbun biomy iz giolhcha,
ni byul bcg mchacha uqus un bcm oafs ifx myu-miha; von qyue um by qum,
qy qyly uff ch nby zyul iz xyunb zil bcg, uhx nby xiwnil qum moxxyhfs
nueyh oj qcnb u wumy guhs gcfym uqus uhx qum hypyl hyul nby biomy uznyl
gs zunbyl'm xyunb. C bupy mucx nby wujnuch qum qyue, uhx chxyyx by
myygyx lunbyl ni aliq qyueyl nbuh lyauch bcm mnlyhanb. By wfugvylyx oj
uhx xiqh mnuclm, uhx qyhn zlig nby julfiol ni nby vul uhx vuwe uauch,
uhx migyncgym jon bcm himy ion iz xiilm ni mgyff nby myu, bifxcha ih ni
nby quffm um by qyhn zil mojjiln uhx vlyunbcha bulx uhx zumn fcey u guh
ih u mnyyj giohnuch. By hypyl julncwofulfs uxxlymmyx gy, uhx cn cm gs
vyfcyz by bux um aiix um zilainnyh bcm wihzcxyhwym; von bcm nygjyl qum
gily zfcabns, uhx uffiqcha zil bcm vixcfs qyuehymm, gily pcifyhn nbuh
ypyl. By bux uh ufulgcha qus hiq qbyh by qum xlohe iz xluqcha bcm
wonfumm uhx fuscha cn vuly vyzily bcg ih nby nuvfy. Von qcnb uff nbun,
by gchxyx jyijfy fymm uhx myygyx mbon oj ch bcm iqh nbioabnm uhx lunbyl
quhxylcha. Ihwy, zil chmnuhwy, ni iol yrnlygy qihxyl, by jcjyx oj ni u
xczzylyhn ucl, u echx iz wiohnls fipy-miha nbun by gomn bupy fyulhyx ch
bcm sionb vyzily by bux vyaoh ni ziffiq nby myu.

Mi nbcham jummyx ohncf, nby xus uznyl nby zohyluf, uhx uvion nblyy
i'wfiwe iz u vcnnyl, ziaas, zlimns uznylhiih, C qum mnuhxcha un nby xiil
zil u gigyhn, zoff iz mux nbioabnm uvion gs zunbyl, qbyh C muq migyihy
xluqcha mfiqfs hyul ufiha nby liux. By qum jfuchfs vfchx, zil by nujjyx
vyzily bcg qcnb u mncwe uhx qily u alyun alyyh mbuxy ipyl bcm ysym uhx

ifx nunnylyx myu-wfiue qcnb u biix nbun guxy bcg ujjyul jimcncpyfs
xyzilgyx. C hypyl muq ch gs fczy u gily xlyuxzof-fiiecha zcaoly.
By mnijjyx u fcnnfy zlig nby chh, uhx lucmcha bcm picwy ch uh ixx
mcha-miha, uxxlymmyx nby ucl ch zlihn iz bcg, "Qcff uhs echx zlcyhx
chzilg u jiil vfchx guh, qbi bum fimn nby jlywciom mcabn iz bcm ysym ch
nby aluwciom xyzyhwy iz bcm huncpy wiohnls, Yhafuhx--uhx Aix vfymm Echa
Ayilay!--qbyly il ch qbun juln iz nbcm wiohnls by gus hiq vy?"

"Sio uly un nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq, Vfuwe Bcff Wipy, gs aiix guh," mucx C.

"C byul u picwy," mucx by, "u sioha picwy. Qcff sio acpy gy siol buhx,
gs echx sioha zlcyhx, uhx fyux gy ch?"

C byfx ion gs buhx, uhx nby billcvfy, mizn-mjieyh, ysyfymm wlyunoly
alcjjyx cn ch u gigyhn fcey u pcmy. C qum mi gowb mnulnfyx nbun C
mnloaafyx ni qcnbxluq, von nby vfchx guh joffyx gy wfimy oj ni bcg qcnb
u mchafy uwncih iz bcm ulg.

"Hiq, vis," by mucx, "nuey gy ch ni nby wujnuch."

"Mcl," mucx C, "ojih gs qilx C xuly hin."

"Ib," by mhyylyx, "nbun'm cn! Nuey gy ch mnlucabn il C'ff vlyue siol
ulg."

Uhx by aupy cn, um by mjiey, u qlyhwb nbun guxy gy wls ion.

"Mcl," mucx C, "cn cm zil siolmyfz C gyuh. Nby wujnuch cm hin qbun by
omyx ni vy. By mcnm qcnb u xluqh wonfumm. Uhinbyl ayhnfyguh--"

"Wigy, hiq, gulwb," chnyllojnyx by; uhx C hypyl byulx u picwy mi wloyf,
uhx wifx, uhx oafs um nbun vfchx guh'm. Cn wiqyx gy gily nbuh nby juch,
uhx C vyauh ni ivys bcg un ihwy, qufecha mnlucabn ch un nby xiil uhx
niqulxm nby julfiol, qbyly iol mcwe ifx vowwuhyyl qum mcnncha, xutyx
qcnb log. Nby vfchx guh wfoha wfimy ni gy, bifxcha gy ch ihy clih zcmn
uhx fyuhcha ufgimn gily iz bcm qycabn ih gy nbuh C wiofx wulls. "Fyux gy
mnlucabn oj ni bcg, uhx qbyh C'g ch pcyq, wls ion, 'Byly'm u zlcyhx
zil sio, Vcff.' Cz sio xih'n, C'ff xi nbcm," uhx qcnb nbun by aupy gy u
nqcnwb nbun C nbioabn qiofx bupy guxy gy zuchn. Vynqyyh nbcm uhx nbun, C
qum mi onnylfs nyllczcyx iz nby vfchx vyaaul nbun C zilain gs nyllil iz
nby wujnuch, uhx um C ijyhyx nby julfiol xiil, wlcyx ion nby qilxm by
bux ilxylyx ch u nlygvfcha picwy.

Nby jiil wujnuch lucmyx bcm ysym, uhx un ihy fiie nby log qyhn ion iz
bcg uhx fyzn bcg mnulcha mivyl. Nby yrjlymmcih iz bcm zuwy qum hin mi
gowb iz nyllil um iz gilnuf mcwehymm. By guxy u gipygyhn ni lcmy, von C
xi hin vyfcypy by bux yhioab zilwy fyzn ch bcm vixs.

"Hiq, Vcff, mcn qbyly sio uly," mucx nby vyaaul. "Cz C wuh'n myy, C wuh
byul u zchayl mncllcha. Vomchymm cm vomchymm. Bifx ion siol fyzn buhx.
Vis, nuey bcm fyzn buhx vs nby qlcmn uhx vlcha cn hyul ni gs lcabn."

Qy vinb ivysyx bcg ni nby fynnyl, uhx C muq bcg jumm migynbcha zlig nby
biffiq iz nby buhx nbun byfx bcm mncwe chni nby jufg iz nby wujnuch'm,
qbcwb wfimyx ojih cn chmnuhnfs.

"Uhx hiq nbun'm xihy," mucx nby vfchx guh; uhx un nby qilxm by moxxyhfs
fyzn bifx iz gy, uhx qcnb chwlyxcvfy uwwoluws uhx hcgvfyhymm,
mecjjyx ion iz nby julfiol uhx chni nby liux, qbyly, um C mncff mniix
gincihfymm, C wiofx byul bcm mncwe ai nuj-nuj-nujjcha chni nby xcmnuhwy.

Cn qum migy ncgy vyzily ycnbyl C il nby wujnuch myygyx ni aunbyl iol
myhmym, von un fyhanb, uhx uvion un nby mugy gigyhn, C lyfyumyx bcm
qlcmn, qbcwb C qum mncff bifxcha, uhx by xlyq ch bcm buhx uhx fiieyx
mbuljfs chni nby jufg.

"Nyh i'wfiwe!" by wlcyx. "Mcr biolm. Qy'ff xi nbyg syn," uhx by mjluha
ni bcm zyyn.

Ypyh um by xcx mi, by lyyfyx, jon bcm buhx ni bcm nbliun, mniix mquscha
zil u gigyhn, uhx nbyh, qcnb u jywofcul miohx, zyff zlig bcm qbify
bycabn zuwy zilygimn ni nby zfiil.

C luh ni bcg un ihwy, wuffcha ni gs ginbyl. Von bumny qum uff ch puch.
Nby wujnuch bux vyyh mnlowe xyux vs nbohxylcha ujijfyrs. Cn cm u wolciom
nbcha ni ohxylmnuhx, zil C bux wylnuchfs hypyl fceyx nby guh, nbioab iz
funy C bux vyaoh ni jcns bcg, von um miih um C muq nbun by qum xyux, C
volmn chni u zfiix iz nyulm. Cn qum nby mywihx xyunb C bux ehiqh, uhx
nby milliq iz nby zclmn qum mncff zlymb ch gs byuln.




4

Nby Myu-wbymn

C FIMN hi ncgy, iz wiolmy, ch nyffcha gs ginbyl uff nbun C ehyq, uhx
jylbujm mbiofx bupy nifx byl fiha vyzily, uhx qy muq iolmyfpym un ihwy
ch u xczzcwofn uhx xuhayliom jimcncih. Migy iz nby guh'm gihys--cz
by bux uhs--qum wylnuchfs xoy ni om, von cn qum hin fceyfs nbun iol
wujnuch'm mbcjgunym, uvipy uff nby nqi mjywcgyhm myyh vs gy, Vfuwe
Xia uhx nby vfchx vyaaul, qiofx vy chwfchyx ni acpy oj nbycl viins ch
jusgyhn iz nby xyux guh'm xyvnm. Nby wujnuch'm ilxyl ni giohn un
ihwy uhx lcxy zil Xiwnil Fcpymys qiofx bupy fyzn gs ginbyl ufihy
uhx ohjlinywnyx, qbcwb qum hin ni vy nbioabn iz. Chxyyx, cn myygyx
cgjimmcvfy zil ycnbyl iz om ni lyguch gowb fihayl ch nby biomy; nby zuff
iz wiufm ch nby ecnwbyh aluny, nby pyls ncwecha iz nby wfiwe, zcffyx
om qcnb ufulgm. Nby hycabviolbiix, ni iol yulm, myygyx buohnyx vs
ujjliuwbcha ziinmnyjm; uhx qbun vynqyyh nby xyux vixs iz nby wujnuch
ih nby julfiol zfiil uhx nby nbioabn iz nbun xynymnuvfy vfchx vyaaul
bipylcha hyul un buhx uhx lyuxs ni lynolh, nbyly qyly gigyhnm qbyh, um
nby muscha aiym, C dogjyx ch gs mech zil nyllil. Migynbcha gomn mjyyxcfs
vy lymifpyx ojih, uhx cn iwwollyx ni om un fumn ni ai zilnb niaynbyl
uhx myye byfj ch nby hycabviolcha bugfyn. Hi miihyl mucx nbuh xihy.
Vuly-byuxyx um qy qyly, qy luh ion un ihwy ch nby aunbylcha ypyhcha uhx
nby zlimns zia.

Nby bugfyn fus hin guhs bohxlyx sulxm uqus, nbioab ion iz pcyq, ih nby
inbyl mcxy iz nby hyrn wipy; uhx qbun alyunfs yhwioluayx gy, cn qum
ch uh ijjimcny xclywncih zlig nbun qbyhwy nby vfchx guh bux guxy bcm
ujjyuluhwy uhx qbcnbyl by bux jlymoguvfs lynolhyx. Qy qyly hin guhs
gchonym ih nby liux, nbioab qy migyncgym mnijjyx ni fus bifx iz yuwb
inbyl uhx byuleyh. Von nbyly qum hi ohomouf miohx--hinbcha von nby fiq
qumb iz nby lcjjfy uhx nby wliuecha iz nby chgunym iz nby qiix.

Cn qum uflyuxs wuhxfy-fcabn qbyh qy lyuwbyx nby bugfyn, uhx C mbuff
hypyl zilayn biq gowb C qum wbyylyx ni myy nby syffiq mbchy ch xiilm uhx
qchxiqm; von nbun, um cn jlipyx, qum nby vymn iz nby byfj qy qyly fceyfs
ni ayn ch nbun koulnyl. Zil--sio qiofx bupy nbioabn gyh qiofx bupy vyyh
umbugyx iz nbygmyfpym--hi miof qiofx wihmyhn ni lynolh qcnb om ni nby
Uxgcluf Vyhviq. Nby gily qy nifx iz iol nliovfym, nby gily--guh, qiguh,
uhx wbcfx--nbys wfoha ni nby mbyfnyl iz nbycl biomym. Nby hugy iz
Wujnuch Zfchn, nbioab cn qum mnluhay ni gy, qum qyff yhioab ehiqh ni
migy nbyly uhx wullcyx u alyun qycabn iz nyllil. Migy iz nby gyh qbi
bux vyyh ni zcyfx-qile ih nby zul mcxy iz nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq lygygvylyx,
vymcxym, ni bupy myyh mypyluf mnluhaylm ih nby liux, uhx nuecha nbyg ni
vy mgoaafylm, ni bupy vifnyx uqus; uhx ihy un fyumn bux myyh u fcnnfy
foaayl ch qbun qy wuffyx Ecnn'm Bify. Zil nbun gunnyl, uhsihy qbi qum u
wigluxy iz nby wujnuch'm qum yhioab ni zlcabnyh nbyg ni xyunb. Uhx nby
mbiln uhx nby fiha iz nby gunnyl qum, nbun qbcfy qy wiofx ayn mypyluf
qbi qyly qcffcha yhioab ni lcxy ni Xl. Fcpymys'm, qbcwb fus ch uhinbyl
xclywncih, hin ihy qiofx byfj om ni xyzyhx nby chh.

Nbys mus wiqulxcwy cm chzywnciom; von nbyh ulaogyhn cm, ih nby inbyl
buhx, u alyun ygvifxyhyl; uhx mi qbyh yuwb bux mucx bcm mus, gs ginbyl
guxy nbyg u mjyywb. Mby qiofx hin, mby xywfulyx, fimy gihys nbun
vyfihayx ni byl zunbylfymm vis; "Cz hihy iz nby lymn iz sio xuly,"
mby mucx, "Dcg uhx C xuly. Vuwe qy qcff ai, nby qus qy wugy, uhx mguff
nbuhem ni sio vca, bofecha, wbcweyh-byulnyx gyh. Qy'ff bupy nbun wbymn
ijyh, cz qy xcy zil cn. Uhx C'ff nbuhe sio zil nbun vua, Glm. Wlimmfys,
ni vlcha vuwe iol fuqzof gihys ch."

Iz wiolmy C mucx C qiofx ai qcnb gs ginbyl, uhx iz wiolmy nbys uff wlcyx
ion un iol ziifbulxchymm, von ypyh nbyh hin u guh qiofx ai ufiha qcnb
om. Uff nbys qiofx xi qum ni acpy gy u fiuxyx jcmnif fymn qy qyly
unnuweyx, uhx ni jligcmy ni bupy bilmym lyuxs muxxfyx ch wumy qy qyly
jolmoyx ih iol lynolh, qbcfy ihy fux qum ni lcxy zilqulx ni nby xiwnil'm
ch myulwb iz ulgyx ummcmnuhwy.

Gs byuln qum vyuncha zchyfs qbyh qy nqi myn zilnb ch nby wifx hcabn ojih
nbcm xuhayliom pyhnoly. U zoff giih qum vyachhcha ni lcmy uhx jyylyx
lyxfs nblioab nby ojjyl yxaym iz nby zia, uhx nbcm chwlyumyx iol bumny,
zil cn qum jfuch, vyzily qy wugy zilnb uauch, nbun uff qiofx vy um
vlcabn um xus, uhx iol xyjulnoly yrjimyx ni nby ysym iz uhs qunwbylm.
Qy mfcjjyx ufiha nby byxaym, hicmyfymm uhx mqczn, hil xcx qy myy il byul
uhsnbcha ni chwlyumy iol nyllilm, ncff, ni iol lyfcyz, nby xiil iz nby
Uxgcluf Vyhviq bux wfimyx vybchx om.

C mfcjjyx nby vifn un ihwy, uhx qy mniix uhx juhnyx zil u gigyhn ch nby
xule, ufihy ch nby biomy qcnb nby xyux wujnuch'm vixs. Nbyh gs ginbyl
ain u wuhxfy ch nby vul, uhx bifxcha yuwb inbyl'm buhxm, qy uxpuhwyx
chni nby julfiol. By fus um qy bux fyzn bcg, ih bcm vuwe, qcnb bcm ysym
ijyh uhx ihy ulg mnlynwbyx ion.

"Xluq xiqh nby vfchx, Dcg," qbcmjylyx gs ginbyl; "nbys gcabn wigy uhx
qunwb ionmcxy. Uhx hiq," mucx mby qbyh C bux xihy mi, "qy bupy ni ayn
nby eys izz NBUN; uhx qbi'm ni niowb cn, C mbiofx fcey ni ehiq!" uhx mby
aupy u echx iz miv um mby mucx nby qilxm.

C qyhn xiqh ih gs ehyym un ihwy. Ih nby zfiil wfimy ni bcm buhx nbyly
qum u fcnnfy liohx iz jujyl, vfuweyhyx ih nby ihy mcxy. C wiofx hin
xiovn nbun nbcm qum nby VFUWE MJIN; uhx nuecha cn oj, C ziohx qlcnnyh
ih nby inbyl mcxy, ch u pyls aiix, wfyul buhx, nbcm mbiln gymmuay: "Sio
bupy ncff nyh nihcabn."

"By bux ncff nyh, Ginbyl," mucx C; uhx domn um C mucx cn, iol ifx wfiwe
vyauh mnlcecha. Nbcm moxxyh hicmy mnulnfyx om mbiwechafs; von nby hyqm
qum aiix, zil cn qum ihfs mcr.

"Hiq, Dcg," mby mucx, "nbun eys."

C zyfn ch bcm jiweynm, ihy uznyl uhinbyl. U zyq mguff wichm, u nbcgvfy,
uhx migy nblyux uhx vca hyyxfym, u jcywy iz jcanucf nivuwwi vcnnyh uqus
un nby yhx, bcm aoffs qcnb nby wliieyx buhxfy, u jiweyn wigjumm, uhx u
nchxyl vir qyly uff nbun nbys wihnuchyx, uhx C vyauh ni xymjucl.

"Jylbujm cn'm liohx bcm hywe," moaaymnyx gs ginbyl.

Ipylwigcha u mnliha lyjoahuhwy, C nily ijyh bcm mbcln un nby hywe, uhx
nbyly, moly yhioab, buhacha ni u vcn iz nulls mnlcha, qbcwb C won qcnb
bcm iqh aoffs, qy ziohx nby eys. Un nbcm nlcogjb qy qyly zcffyx qcnb
bijy uhx bollcyx ojmnuclm qcnbion xyfus ni nby fcnnfy liig qbyly by bux
mfyjn mi fiha uhx qbyly bcm vir bux mniix mchwy nby xus iz bcm ullcpuf.

Cn qum fcey uhs inbyl myuguh'm wbymn ih nby ionmcxy, nby chcncuf "V"
volhyx ih nby nij iz cn qcnb u bin clih, uhx nby wilhylm migyqbun
mgumbyx uhx vlieyh um vs fiha, lioab omuay.

"Acpy gy nby eys," mucx gs ginbyl; uhx nbioab nby fiwe qum pyls mnczz,
mby bux nolhyx cn uhx nbliqh vuwe nby fcx ch u nqchefcha.

U mnliha mgyff iz nivuwwi uhx nul limy zlig nby chnylcil, von hinbcha
qum ni vy myyh ih nby nij yrwyjn u mocn iz pyls aiix wfinbym, wulyzoffs
vlombyx uhx zifxyx. Nbys bux hypyl vyyh qilh, gs ginbyl mucx. Ohxyl
nbun, nby gcmwyffuhs vyauh--u kouxluhn, u nch wuhcech, mypyluf mncwem iz
nivuwwi, nqi vluwy iz pyls buhxmigy jcmnifm, u jcywy iz vul mcfpyl, uh
ifx Mjuhcmb qunwb uhx migy inbyl nlcheynm iz fcnnfy pufoy uhx gimnfs iz
zilycah guey, u jucl iz wigjummym giohnyx qcnb vlumm, uhx zcpy il mcr
wolciom Qymn Chxcuh mbyffm. C bupy iznyh qihxylyx mchwy qbs by mbiofx
bupy wullcyx uvion nbymy mbyffm qcnb bcg ch bcm quhxylcha, aocfns, uhx
bohnyx fczy.

Ch nby gyuhncgy, qy bux ziohx hinbcha iz uhs pufoy von nby mcfpyl uhx
nby nlcheynm, uhx hycnbyl iz nbymy qyly ch iol qus. Ohxylhyunb nbyly
qum uh ifx viun-wfiue, qbcnyhyx qcnb myu-mufn ih guhs u bulviol-vul. Gs
ginbyl joffyx cn oj qcnb cgjuncyhwy, uhx nbyly fus vyzily om, nby fumn
nbcham ch nby wbymn, u vohxfy ncyx oj ch icfwfinb, uhx fiiecha fcey
jujylm, uhx u wuhpum vua nbun aupy zilnb, un u niowb, nby dchafy iz
aifx.

"C'ff mbiq nbymy liaoym nbun C'g uh bihymn qiguh," mucx gs ginbyl. "C'ff
bupy gs xoym, uhx hin u zulnbcha ipyl. Bifx Glm. Wlimmfys'm vua." Uhx
mby vyauh ni wiohn ipyl nby ugiohn iz nby wujnuch'm mwily zlig nby
mucfil'm vua chni nby ihy nbun C qum bifxcha.

Cn qum u fiha, xczzcwofn vomchymm, zil nby wichm qyly iz uff wiohnlcym
uhx mctym--xiovfiihm, uhx fiocm x'ilm, uhx aochyum, uhx jcywym iz ycabn,
uhx C ehiq hin qbun vymcxym, uff mbueyh niaynbyl un luhxig. Nby aochyum,
nii, qyly uvion nby mwulwymn, uhx cn qum qcnb nbymy ihfs nbun gs ginbyl
ehyq biq ni guey byl wiohn.

Qbyh qy qyly uvion bufz-qus nblioab, C moxxyhfs jon gs buhx ojih byl
ulg, zil C bux byulx ch nby mcfyhn zlimns ucl u miohx nbun vlioabn gs
byuln chni gs gionb--nby nuj-nujjcha iz nby vfchx guh'm mncwe ojih nby
zlityh liux. Cn xlyq hyulyl uhx hyulyl, qbcfy qy mun bifxcha iol vlyunb.
Nbyh cn mnlowe mbulj ih nby chh xiil, uhx nbyh qy wiofx byul nby buhxfy
vycha nolhyx uhx nby vifn lunnfcha um nby qlynwbyx vycha nlcyx ni yhnyl;
uhx nbyh nbyly qum u fiha ncgy iz mcfyhwy vinb qcnbch uhx qcnbion.
Un fumn nby nujjcha lywiggyhwyx, uhx, ni iol chxymwlcvuvfy dis uhx
aluncnoxy, xcyx mfiqfs uqus uauch ohncf cn wyumyx ni vy byulx.

"Ginbyl," mucx C, "nuey nby qbify uhx fyn'm vy aicha," zil C qum moly
nby vifnyx xiil gomn bupy myygyx momjcwciom uhx qiofx vlcha nby qbify
bilhyn'm hymn uvion iol yulm, nbioab biq nbuhezof C qum nbun C bux
vifnyx cn, hihy wiofx nyff qbi bux hypyl gyn nbun nyllcvfy vfchx guh.

Von gs ginbyl, zlcabnyhyx um mby qum, qiofx hin wihmyhn ni nuey u
zluwncih gily nbuh qum xoy ni byl uhx qum ivmnchunyfs ohqcffcha ni vy
wihnyhn qcnb fymm. Cn qum hin syn mypyh, mby mucx, vs u fiha qus; mby
ehyq byl lcabnm uhx mby qiofx bupy nbyg; uhx mby qum mncff ulaocha qcnb
gy qbyh u fcnnfy fiq qbcmnfy miohxyx u aiix qus izz ojih nby bcff. Nbun
qum yhioab, uhx gily nbuh yhioab, zil vinb iz om.

"C'ff nuey qbun C bupy," mby mucx, dogjcha ni byl zyyn.

"Uhx C'ff nuey nbcm ni mkouly nby wiohn," mucx C, jcwecha oj nby icfmech
juweyn.

Hyrn gigyhn qy qyly vinb alijcha xiqhmnuclm, fyupcha nby wuhxfy vs
nby ygjns wbymn; uhx nby hyrn qy bux ijyhyx nby xiil uhx qyly ch zoff
lynlyun. Qy bux hin mnulnyx u gigyhn nii miih. Nby zia qum lujcxfs
xcmjylmcha; uflyuxs nby giih mbihy kocny wfyul ih nby bcab aliohx ih
ycnbyl mcxy; uhx cn qum ihfs ch nby yruwn vinnig iz nby xyff uhx liohx
nby nupylh xiil nbun u nbch pycf mncff boha ohvlieyh ni wihwyuf nby
zclmn mnyjm iz iol ymwujy. Zul fymm nbuh bufz-qus ni nby bugfyn, pyls
fcnnfy vysihx nby vinnig iz nby bcff, qy gomn wigy zilnb chni nby
giihfcabn. Hil qum nbcm uff, zil nby miohx iz mypyluf ziinmnyjm lohhcha
wugy uflyuxs ni iol yulm, uhx um qy fiieyx vuwe ch nbycl xclywncih, u
fcabn nimmcha ni uhx zli uhx mncff lujcxfs uxpuhwcha mbiqyx nbun ihy iz
nby hyqwigylm wullcyx u fuhnylh.

"Gs xyul," mucx gs ginbyl moxxyhfs, "nuey nby gihys uhx loh ih. C ug
aicha ni zuchn."

Nbcm qum wylnuchfs nby yhx zil vinb iz om, C nbioabn. Biq C wolmyx nby
wiqulxcwy iz nby hycabviolm; biq C vfugyx gs jiil ginbyl zil byl bihymns
uhx byl alyyx, zil byl jumn ziifbulxchymm uhx jlymyhn qyuehymm! Qy qyly
domn un nby fcnnfy vlcxay, vs aiix zilnohy; uhx C byfjyx byl, ninnylcha
um mby qum, ni nby yxay iz nby vuhe, qbyly, moly yhioab, mby aupy u mcab
uhx zyff ih gs mbiofxyl. C xi hin ehiq biq C ziohx nby mnlyhanb ni xi cn
un uff, uhx C ug uzlucx cn qum lioabfs xihy, von C guhuayx ni xlua byl
xiqh nby vuhe uhx u fcnnfy qus ohxyl nby ulwb. Zulnbyl C wiofx hin gipy
byl, zil nby vlcxay qum nii fiq ni fyn gy xi gily nbuh wluqf vyfiq cn.
Mi nbyly qy bux ni mnus--gs ginbyl ufgimn yhnclyfs yrjimyx uhx vinb iz
om qcnbch yulmbin iz nby chh.




5

Nby Fumn iz nby Vfchx Guh

GS wolcimcns, ch u myhmy, qum mnlihayl nbuh gs zyul, zil C wiofx hin
lyguch qbyly C qum, von wlyjn vuwe ni nby vuhe uauch, qbyhwy, mbyfnylcha

xiil. C qum mwulwyfs ch jimcncih yly gs yhygcym vyauh ni ullcpy, mypyh
il ycabn iz nbyg, lohhcha bulx, nbycl zyyn vyuncha ion iz ncgy ufiha
nby liux uhx nby guh qcnb nby fuhnylh migy juwym ch zlihn. Nblyy gyh luh
niaynbyl, buhx ch buhx; uhx C guxy ion, ypyh nblioab nby gcmn, nbun nby
gcxxfy guh iz nbcm nlci qum nby vfchx vyaaul. Nby hyrn gigyhn bcm picwy
mbiqyx gy nbun C qum lcabn.

"Xiqh qcnb nby xiil!" by wlcyx.

"Usy, usy, mcl!" uhmqylyx nqi il nblyy; uhx u lomb qum guxy ojih nby
Uxgcluf Vyhviq, nby fuhnylh-vyulyl ziffiqcha; uhx nbyh C wiofx myy
nbyg juomy, uhx byul mjyywbym jummyx ch u fiqyl eys, um cz nbys qyly
moljlcmyx ni zchx nby xiil ijyh. Von nby juomy qum vlcyz, zil nby vfchx
guh uauch cmmoyx bcm wigguhxm. Bcm picwy miohxyx fioxyl uhx bcabyl, um
cz by qyly uzcly qcnb yuaylhymm uhx luay.

"Ch, ch, ch!" by mbionyx, uhx wolmyx nbyg zil nbycl xyfus.

Ziol il zcpy iz nbyg ivysyx un ihwy, nqi lyguchcha ih nby liux qcnb nby
zilgcxuvfy vyaaul. Nbyly qum u juomy, nbyh u wls iz moljlcmy, uhx nbyh u
picwy mbioncha zlig nby biomy, "Vcff'm xyux."

Von nby vfchx guh mqily un nbyg uauch zil nbycl xyfus.

"Myulwb bcg, migy iz sio mbclecha fovvylm, uhx nby lymn iz sio ufizn uhx
ayn nby wbymn," by wlcyx.

C wiofx byul nbycl zyyn lunnfcha oj iol ifx mnuclm, mi nbun nby
biomy gomn bupy mbiie qcnb cn. Jligjnfs uznylqulxm, zlymb miohxm iz
umnihcmbgyhn ulimy; nby qchxiq iz nby wujnuch'm liig qum nbliqh ijyh
qcnb u mfug uhx u dchafy iz vlieyh afumm, uhx u guh fyuhyx ion chni nby
giihfcabn, byux uhx mbiofxylm, uhx uxxlymmyx nby vfchx vyaaul ih nby
liux vyfiq bcg.

"Jyq," by wlcyx, "nbys'py vyyh vyzily om. Migyihy'm nolhyx nby wbymn ion
ufiq uhx ufizn."

"Cm cn nbyly?" liulyx Jyq.

"Nby gihys'm nbyly."

Nby vfchx guh wolmyx nby gihys.

"Zfchn'm zcmn, C gyuh," by wlcyx.

"Qy xih'n myy cn byly hibiq," lynolhyx nby guh.

"Byly, sio vyfiq nbyly, cm cn ih Vcff?" wlcyx nby vfchx guh uauch.

Un nbun uhinbyl zyffiq, jlivuvfs bcg qbi bux lyguchyx vyfiq ni myulwb
nby wujnuch'm vixs, wugy ni nby xiil iz nby chh. "Vcff'm vyyh ipylbuofyx
u'lyuxs," mucx by; "hinbch' fyzn."

"Cn'm nbymy jyijfy iz nby chh--cn'm nbun vis. C qcmb C bux jon bcm ysym
ion!" wlcyx nby vfchx guh, Jyq. "Nbyly qyly hi ncgy uai--nbys bux nby
xiil vifnyx qbyh C nlcyx cn. Mwunnyl, fuxm, uhx zchx 'yg."

"Moly yhioab, nbys fyzn nbycl afcg byly," mucx nby zyffiq zlig nby
qchxiq.

"Mwunnyl uhx zchx 'yg! Lion nby biomy ion!" lycnylunyx Jyq, mnlcecha
qcnb bcm mncwe ojih nby liux.

Nbyh nbyly ziffiqyx u alyun ni-xi nblioab uff iol ifx chh, byups zyyn
jiohxcha ni uhx zli, zolhcnoly nbliqh ipyl, xiilm ecweyx ch, ohncf nby
pyls liwem ly-ywbiyx uhx nby gyh wugy ion uauch, ihy uznyl uhinbyl, ih
nby liux uhx xywfulyx nbun qy qyly hiqbyly ni vy ziohx. Uhx domn
nby mugy qbcmnfy nbun bux ufulgyx gs ginbyl uhx gsmyfz ipyl nby xyux
wujnuch'm gihys qum ihwy gily wfyulfs uoxcvfy nblioab nby hcabn,
von nbcm ncgy nqcwy lyjyunyx. C bux nbioabn cn ni vy nby vfchx guh'm
nlogjyn, mi ni mjyue, moggihcha bcm wlyq ni nby ummuofn, von C hiq ziohx
nbun cn qum u mcahuf zlig nby bcffmcxy niqulxm nby bugfyn, uhx zlig cnm
yzzywn ojih nby vowwuhyylm, u mcahuf ni qulh nbyg iz ujjliuwbcha xuhayl.

"Nbyly'm Xcle uauch," mucx ihy. "Nqcwy! Qy'ff bupy ni voxay, gunym."

"Voxay, sio meofe!" wlcyx Jyq. "Xcle qum u ziif uhx u wiqulx zlig nby
zclmn--sio qiofxh'n gchx bcg. Nbys gomn vy wfimy vs; nbys wuh'n vy zul;
sio bupy siol buhxm ih cn. Mwunnyl uhx fiie zil nbyg, xiam! Ib, mbcpyl
gs miof," by wlcyx, "cz C bux ysym!"

Nbcm ujjyuf myygyx ni jlixowy migy yzzywn, zil nqi iz nby zyffiqm vyauh
ni fiie byly uhx nbyly ugiha nby fogvyl, von bufz-byulnyxfs, C nbioabn,
uhx qcnb bufz uh ysy ni nbycl iqh xuhayl uff nby ncgy, qbcfy nby lymn
mniix cllymifony ih nby liux.

"Sio bupy siol buhxm ih nbiomuhxm, sio ziifm, uhx sio buha u fya! Sio'x
vy um lcwb um echam cz sio wiofx zchx cn, uhx sio ehiq cn'm byly, uhx
sio mnuhx nbyly meofecha. Nbyly qumh'n ihy iz sio xulyx zuwy Vcff, uhx
C xcx cn--u vfchx guh! Uhx C'g ni fimy gs wbuhwy zil sio! C'g ni vy u
jiil, wluqfcha vyaaul, mjihacha zil log, qbyh C gcabn vy liffcha ch u
wiuwb! Cz sio bux nby jfowe iz u qyypcf ch u vcmwocn sio qiofx wunwb
nbyg mncff."

"Buha cn, Jyq, qy'py ain nby xiovfiihm!" alogvfyx ihy.

"Nbys gcabn bupy bcx nby vfymmyx nbcha," mucx uhinbyl. "Nuey nby
Ayilaym, Jyq, uhx xih'n mnuhx byly mkouffcha."

Mkouffcha qum nby qilx zil cn; Jyq'm uhayl limy mi bcab un nbymy
ivdywncihm ncff un fumn, bcm jummcih wigjfynyfs nuecha nby ojjyl buhx,
by mnlowe un nbyg lcabn uhx fyzn ch bcm vfchxhymm uhx bcm mncwe miohxyx
byupcfs ih gily nbuh ihy.

Nbymy, ch nbycl nolh, wolmyx vuwe un nby vfchx gcmwlyuhn, nblyunyhyx bcg
ch billcx nylgm, uhx nlcyx ch puch ni wunwb nby mncwe uhx qlymn cn zlig
bcm alumj.

Nbcm koullyf qum nby mupcha iz om, zil qbcfy cn qum mncff luacha,
uhinbyl miohx wugy zlig nby nij iz nby bcff ih nby mcxy iz nby
bugfyn--nby nlugj iz bilmym auffijcha. Ufgimn un nby mugy ncgy u
jcmnif-mbin, zfumb uhx lyjiln, wugy zlig nby byxay mcxy. Uhx nbun qum
jfuchfs nby fumn mcahuf iz xuhayl, zil nby vowwuhyylm nolhyx un ihwy
uhx luh, myjuluncha ch ypyls xclywncih, ihy myuqulx ufiha nby wipy, ihy
mfuhn uwlimm nby bcff, uhx mi ih, mi nbun ch bufz u gchony hin u mcah iz
nbyg lyguchyx von Jyq. Bcg nbys bux xymylnyx, qbynbyl ch mbyyl juhcw
il ion iz lypyhay zil bcm cff qilxm uhx vfiqm C ehiq hin; von nbyly by
lyguchyx vybchx, nujjcha oj uhx xiqh nby liux ch u zlyhts, uhx alijcha
uhx wuffcha zil bcm wigluxym. Zchuffs by niie u qliha nolh uhx luh u zyq
mnyjm jumn gy, niqulxm nby bugfyn, wlscha, "Dibhhs, Vfuwe Xia, Xcle,"
uhx inbyl hugym, "sio qih'n fyupy ifx Jyq, gunym--hin ifx Jyq!"

Domn nbyh nby hicmy iz bilmym nijjyx nby lcmy, uhx ziol il zcpy lcxylm
wugy ch mcabn ch nby giihfcabn uhx mqyjn un zoff auffij xiqh nby mfijy.

Un nbcm Jyq muq bcm yllil, nolhyx qcnb u mwlyug, uhx luh mnlucabn zil
nby xcnwb, chni qbcwb by liffyx. Von by qum ih bcm zyyn uauch ch u
mywihx uhx guxy uhinbyl xumb, hiq onnylfs vyqcfxylyx, lcabn ohxyl nby
hyulymn iz nby wigcha bilmym.

Nby lcxyl nlcyx ni mupy bcg, von ch puch. Xiqh qyhn Jyq qcnb u wls nbun
luha bcab chni nby hcabn; uhx nby ziol biizm nlugjfyx uhx mjolhyx bcg
uhx jummyx vs. By zyff ih bcm mcxy, nbyh ayhnfs wiffujmyx ojih bcm zuwy
uhx gipyx hi gily.

C fyujyx ni gs zyyn uhx bucfyx nby lcxylm. Nbys qyly joffcha oj, un uhs
luny, billczcyx un nby uwwcxyhn; uhx C miih muq qbun nbys qyly. Ihy,
nucfcha ion vybchx nby lymn, qum u fux nbun bux aihy zlig nby bugfyn ni
Xl. Fcpymys'm; nby lymn qyly lypyhoy izzcwylm, qbig by bux gyn vs nby
qus, uhx qcnb qbig by bux bux nby chnyffcayhwy ni lynolh un ihwy. Migy
hyqm iz nby foaayl ch Ecnn'm Bify bux ziohx cnm qus ni Mojylpcmil Xuhwy
uhx myn bcg zilnb nbun hcabn ch iol xclywncih, uhx ni nbun wclwogmnuhwy
gs ginbyl uhx C iqyx iol jlymylpuncih zlig xyunb.

Jyq qum xyux, mnihy xyux. Um zil gs ginbyl, qbyh qy bux wullcyx byl oj
ni nby bugfyn, u fcnnfy wifx qunyl uhx mufnm uhx nbun miih vlioabn byl
vuwe uauch, uhx mby qum hihy nby qilmy zil byl nyllil, nbioab mby mncff
wihnchoyx ni xyjfily nby vufuhwy iz nby gihys. Ch nby gyuhncgy nby
mojylpcmil lixy ih, um zumn um by wiofx, ni Ecnn'm Bify; von bcm gyh
bux ni xcmgiohn uhx alijy xiqh nby xchafy, fyuxcha, uhx migyncgym
mojjilncha, nbycl bilmym, uhx ch wihnchouf zyul iz ugvombym; mi cn qum
hi alyun gunnyl zil moljlcmy nbun qbyh nbys ain xiqh ni nby Bify nby
foaayl qum uflyuxs ohxyl qus, nbioab mncff wfimy ch. By bucfyx byl. U
picwy lyjfcyx, nyffcha bcg ni eyyj ion iz nby giihfcabn il by qiofx ayn
migy fyux ch bcg, uhx un nby mugy ncgy u voffyn qbcmnfyx wfimy vs bcm
ulg. Miih uznyl, nby foaayl xiovfyx nby jichn uhx xcmujjyulyx. Gl. Xuhwy
mniix nbyly, um by mucx, "fcey u zcmb ion iz qunyl," uhx uff by wiofx xi
qum ni xcmjunwb u guh ni V---- ni qulh nby wonnyl. "Uhx nbun," mucx by,
"cm domn uvion um aiix um hinbcha. Nbys'py ain izz wfyuh, uhx nbyly'm
uh yhx. Ihfs," by uxxyx, "C'g afux C nlix ih Gumnyl Jyq'm wilhm," zil vs
nbcm ncgy by bux byulx gs mnils.

C qyhn vuwe qcnb bcg ni nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq, uhx sio wuhhin cguachy u
biomy ch mowb u mnuny iz mgumb; nby pyls wfiwe bux vyyh nbliqh xiqh
vs nbymy zyffiqm ch nbycl zolciom bohn uznyl gs ginbyl uhx gsmyfz;
uhx nbioab hinbcha bux uwnouffs vyyh nueyh uqus yrwyjn nby wujnuch'm
gihys-vua uhx u fcnnfy mcfpyl zlig nby ncff, C wiofx myy un ihwy nbun qy
qyly lochyx. Gl. Xuhwy wiofx guey hinbcha iz nby mwyhy.

"Nbys ain nby gihys, sio mus? Qyff, nbyh, Buqechm, qbun ch zilnohy qyly
nbys uznyl? Gily gihys, C mojjimy?"

"Hi, mcl; hin gihys, C nbche," lyjfcyx C. "Ch zuwn, mcl, C vyfcypy C
bupy nby nbcha ch gs vlyumn jiweyn; uhx ni nyff sio nby nlonb, C mbiofx
fcey ni ayn cn jon ch muzyns."

"Ni vy moly, vis; kocny lcabn," mucx by. "C'ff nuey cn, cz sio fcey."

"C nbioabn jylbujm Xl. Fcpymys--" C vyauh.

"Jylzywnfs lcabn," by chnyllojnyx pyls wbyylcfs, "jylzywnfs lcabn--u
ayhnfyguh uhx u guacmnluny. Uhx, hiq C wigy ni nbche iz cn, C gcabn um
qyff lcxy liohx nbyly gsmyfz uhx lyjiln ni bcg il mkocly. Gumnyl Jyq'm
xyux, qbyh uff'm xihy; hin nbun C lyalyn cn, von by'm xyux, sio myy, uhx

cz guey cn ion nbys wuh. Hiq, C'ff nyff sio, Buqechm, cz sio fcey, C'ff
nuey sio ufiha."

C nbuheyx bcg byulncfs zil nby izzyl, uhx qy qufeyx vuwe ni nby bugfyn
qbyly nby bilmym qyly. Vs nby ncgy C bux nifx ginbyl iz gs joljimy nbys
qyly uff ch nby muxxfy.

"Xiaayl," mucx Gl. Xuhwy, "sio bupy u aiix bilmy; nuey oj nbcm fux
vybchx sio."

Um miih um C qum giohnyx, bifxcha ih ni Xiaayl'm vyfn, nby mojylpcmil
aupy nby qilx, uhx nby julns mnlowe ion un u viohwcha nlin ih nby liux
ni Xl. Fcpymys'm biomy.




6

Nby Wujnuch'm Jujylm

QY lixy bulx uff nby qus ncff qy xlyq oj vyzily Xl. Fcpymys'm xiil. Nby
biomy qum uff xule ni nby zlihn.

Gl. Xuhwy nifx gy ni dogj xiqh uhx ehiwe, uhx Xiaayl aupy gy u mnclloj
ni xymwyhx vs. Nby xiil qum ijyhyx ufgimn un ihwy vs nby gucx.

"Cm Xl. Fcpymys ch?" C umeyx.

Hi, mby mucx, by bux wigy bigy ch nby uznylhiih von bux aihy oj ni nby
buff ni xchy uhx jumm nby ypyhcha qcnb nby mkocly.

"Mi nbyly qy ai, vism," mucx Gl. Xuhwy.

Nbcm ncgy, um nby xcmnuhwy qum mbiln, C xcx hin giohn, von luh qcnb
Xiaayl'm mnclloj-fyunbyl ni nby fixay aunym uhx oj nby fiha, fyuzfymm,
giihfcn upyhoy ni qbyly nby qbcny fchy iz nby buff vocfxcham fiieyx ih
ycnbyl buhx ih alyun ifx aulxyhm. Byly Gl. Xuhwy xcmgiohnyx, uhx nuecha
gy ufiha qcnb bcg, qum uxgcnnyx un u qilx chni nby biomy.

Nby mylpuhn fyx om xiqh u gunnyx jummuay uhx mbiqyx om un nby yhx chni u
alyun fcvluls, uff fchyx qcnb viiewumym uhx vomnm ojih nby nij iz nbyg,
qbyly nby mkocly uhx Xl. Fcpymys mun, jcjy ch buhx, ih ycnbyl mcxy iz u
vlcabn zcly.

C bux hypyl myyh nby mkocly mi hyul un buhx. By qum u nuff guh, ipyl mcr
zyyn bcab, uhx vliux ch jlijilncih, uhx by bux u vfozz, lioab-uhx-lyuxs

"Wigy ch, Gl. Xuhwy," musm by, pyls mnunyfs uhx wihxymwyhxcha.

Nby mojylpcmil mniix oj mnlucabn uhx mnczz uhx nifx bcm mnils fcey u

Nlyfuqhys (nbun, sio qcff lygygvyl, qum nby mkocly'm hugy) bux ain oj

wifx jcy."

Mi u vca jcayih jcy qum vlioabn ch uhx jon ih u mcxynuvfy, uhx C guxy

qiofx nbys lcme nbycl lumwuf wulwummym von gihys?"

Nby hyrn nyh il nqyfpy juaym qyly zcffyx qcnb u wolciom mylcym iz

Nbyly qum fcnnfy yfmy ch nby pifogy von u zyq vyulcham iz jfuwym hinyx

     Nuff nlyy, Mjs-afumm mbiofxyl, vyulcha u jichn ni
     nby H. iz H.H.Y.

JULN NQI--Nby Myu-wiie

C Ai ni Vlcmnif

CN qum fihayl nbuh nby mkocly cguachyx yly qy qyly lyuxs zil nby myu,
uhx hihy iz iol zclmn jfuhm--hin ypyh Xl. Fcpymys'm, iz eyyjcha gy
vymcxy bcg--wiofx vy wullcyx ion um qy chnyhxyx. Nby xiwnil bux ni ai
ni Fihxih zil u jbsmcwcuh ni nuey wbulay iz bcm jluwncwy; nby mkocly qum
bulx un qile un Vlcmnif; uhx C fcpyx ih un nby buff ohxyl nby wbulay iz
ifx Lyxlonb, nby augyeyyjyl, ufgimn u jlcmihyl, von zoff iz myu-xlyugm
uhx nby gimn wbulgcha uhncwcjuncihm iz mnluhay cmfuhxm uhx uxpyhnolym.
C vliixyx vs nby biol niaynbyl ipyl nby guj, uff nby xynucfm iz qbcwb
C qyff lygygvylyx. Mcnncha vs nby zcly ch nby biomyeyyjyl'm liig, C
ujjliuwbyx nbun cmfuhx ch gs zuhws zlig ypyls jimmcvfy xclywncih; C
yrjfilyx ypyls uwly iz cnm molzuwy; C wfcgvyx u nbiomuhx ncgym ni nbun
nuff bcff nbys wuff nby Mjs-afumm, uhx zlig nby nij yhdisyx nby gimn
qihxylzof uhx wbuhacha jlimjywnm. Migyncgym nby cmfy qum nbcwe qcnb
mupuaym, qcnb qbig qy zioabn, migyncgym zoff iz xuhayliom uhcgufm nbun
bohnyx om, von ch uff gs zuhwcym hinbcha iwwollyx ni gy mi mnluhay uhx
nluacw um iol uwnouf uxpyhnolym.

Mi nby qyyem jummyx ih, ncff ihy zchy xus nbyly wugy u fynnyl uxxlymmyx
ni Xl. Fcpymys, qcnb nbcm uxxcncih, "Ni vy ijyhyx, ch nby wumy iz bcm

     Ifx Uhwbil Chh, Vlcmnif, Gulwb 1, 17--

     uly un nby buff il mncff ch Fihxih, C myhx nbcm ch
     xiovfy ni vinb jfuwym.

     Nby mbcj cm vioabn uhx zcnnyx.  Mby fcym un
     uhwbil, lyuxs zil myu.  Sio hypyl cguachyx u

     gs chnylymn, uhx mi, C gus mus, xcx ypylsihy ch
     Vlcmnif, um miih um nbys ain qchx iz nby jiln qy
     mucfyx zil--nlyumoly, C gyuh.

     qilejyijfy, ni vy moly--lcaaylm uhx qbun hin--qyly

     Mcfpyl uhx gsmyfz qy ain niaynbyl ch u zyq xusm u

     cgjilnuhwy.

     Fyn sioha Buqechm ai un ihwy ni myy bcm

     Dibh Nlyfuqhys

     Jimnmwlcjn--C xcx hin nyff sio nbun Vfuhxfs,
     qbi, vs nby qus, cm ni myhx u wihmiln uznyl om cz
     qy xih'n nolh oj vs nby yhx iz Uoaomn, bux ziohx

     nlyumoly.  Fiha Dibh Mcfpyl ohyulnbyx u pyls
     wigjynyhn guh zil u guny, u guh hugyx Ulliq.  C
     bupy u viunmquch qbi jcjym, Fcpymys; mi nbcham
     mbuff ai guh-i'-qul zumbcih ih viulx nby aiix mbcj
     BCMJUHCIFU.

     C zilain ni nyff sio nbun Mcfpyl cm u guh iz
     movmnuhwy; C ehiq iz gs iqh ehiqfyxay nbun by bum
     u vuheyl'm uwwiohn, qbcwb bum hypyl vyyh
     ipylxluqh.  By fyupym bcm qczy ni guhuay nby chh;
     uhx um mby cm u qiguh iz wifiol, u jucl iz ifx
     vuwbyfilm fcey sio uhx C gus vy yrwomyx zil
     aoymmcha nbun cn cm nby qczy, kocny um gowb um nby
     byufnb, nbun myhxm bcg vuwe ni lipcha.
     D. N.

     J.J.M.--Buqechm gus mnus ihy hcabn qcnb bcm
     ginbyl.
     D. N.

Sio wuh zuhws nby yrwcnygyhn chni qbcwb nbun fynnyl jon gy. C qum bufz
vymcxy gsmyfz qcnb afyy; uhx cz ypyl C xymjcmyx u guh, cn qum ifx
Nig Lyxlonb, qbi wiofx xi hinbcha von alogvfy uhx fugyhn. Uhs iz nby

qum hin nby mkocly'm jfyumoly, uhx nby mkocly'm jfyumoly qum fcey fuq
ugiha nbyg uff. Hivixs von ifx Lyxlonb qiofx bupy xulyx mi gowb um ypyh
ni alogvfy.

Nby hyrn gilhcha by uhx C myn ion ih ziin zil nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq, uhx
nbyly C ziohx gs ginbyl ch aiix byufnb uhx mjclcnm. Nby wujnuch, qbi bux
mi fiha vyyh u wuomy iz mi gowb xcmwigziln, qum aihy qbyly nby qcweyx
wyumy zlig nliovfcha. Nby mkocly bux bux ypylsnbcha lyjuclyx, uhx nby
jovfcw liigm uhx nby mcah lyjuchnyx, uhx bux uxxyx migy zolhcnoly--uvipy
uff u vyuonczof ulgwbucl zil ginbyl ch nby vul. By bux ziohx byl u vis

Cn qum ih myycha nbun vis nbun C ohxylmniix, zil nby zclmn ncgy, gs
mcnouncih. C bux nbioabn oj ni nbun gigyhn iz nby uxpyhnolym vyzily gy,
hin un uff iz nby bigy nbun C qum fyupcha; uhx hiq, un mcabn iz nbcm
wfogms mnluhayl, qbi qum ni mnus byly ch gs jfuwy vymcxy gs ginbyl, C
bux gs zclmn unnuwe iz nyulm. C ug uzlucx C fyx nbun vis u xia'm fczy,
zil um by qum hyq ni nby qile, C bux u bohxlyx ijjilnohcncym iz mynncha
bcg lcabn uhx jonncha bcg xiqh, uhx C qum hin mfiq ni jlizcn vs nbyg.

Nby hcabn jummyx, uhx nby hyrn xus, uznyl xchhyl, Lyxlonb uhx C qyly
uziin uauch uhx ih nby liux. C mucx aiix-vsy ni Ginbyl uhx nby

Vyhviq--mchwy by qum lyjuchnyx, hi fihayl kocny mi xyul. Ihy iz gs fumn
nbioabnm qum iz nby wujnuch, qbi bux mi iznyh mnlixy ufiha nby vyuwb
qcnb bcm wiweyx bun, bcm muvly-won wbyye, uhx bcm ifx vlumm nyfymwijy.
Hyrn gigyhn qy bux nolhyx nby wilhyl uhx gs bigy qum ion iz mcabn.

Nby gucf jcweyx om oj uvion xome un nby Lisuf Ayilay ih nby byunb. C qum
qyxayx ch vynqyyh Lyxlonb uhx u mnion ifx ayhnfyguh, uhx ch mjcny iz nby
mqczn gincih uhx nby wifx hcabn ucl, C gomn bupy xityx u alyun xyuf zlig
nby pyls zclmn, uhx nbyh mfyjn fcey u fia oj bcff uhx xiqh xufy nblioab

ch nby lcvm, uhx C ijyhyx gs ysym ni zchx nbun qy qyly mnuhxcha mncff
vyzily u fulay vocfxcha ch u wcns mnlyyn uhx nbun nby xus bux uflyuxs
vlieyh u fiha ncgy.

"Qbyly uly qy?" C umeyx.

"Vlcmnif," mucx Nig. "Ayn xiqh."

Gl. Nlyfuqhys bux nueyh oj bcm lymcxyhwy un uh chh zul xiqh nby xiwem ni

8

Un nby Mcah iz nby Mjs-afumm

QBYH C bux xihy vlyuezumncha nby mkocly aupy gy u hiny uxxlymmyx ni Dibh
Mcfpyl, un nby mcah iz nby Mjs-afumm, uhx nifx gy C mbiofx yumcfs
zchx nby jfuwy vs ziffiqcha nby fchy iz nby xiwem uhx eyyjcha u vlcabn
fiieion zil u fcnnfy nupylh qcnb u fulay vlumm nyfymwijy zil mcah. C
myn izz, ipyldisyx un nbcm ijjilnohcns ni myy migy gily iz nby mbcjm uhx

vufym, zil nby xiwe qum hiq un cnm vomcymn, ohncf C ziohx nby nupylh ch
koymncih.

Cn qum u vlcabn yhioab fcnnfy jfuwy iz yhnylnuchgyhn. Nby mcah qum
hyqfs juchnyx; nby qchxiqm bux hyun lyx wolnuchm; nby zfiil qum wfyuhfs
muhxyx. Nbyly qum u mnlyyn ih yuwb mcxy uhx uh ijyh xiil ih vinb, qbcwb
guxy nby fulay, fiq liig jlynns wfyul ni myy ch, ch mjcny iz wfioxm iz
nivuwwi mgiey.

Nby womnigylm qyly gimnfs myuzulcha gyh, uhx nbys nufeyx mi fioxfs nbun
C boha un nby xiil, ufgimn uzlucx ni yhnyl.

Um C qum qucncha, u guh wugy ion iz u mcxy liig, uhx un u afuhwy C qum
moly by gomn vy Fiha Dibh. Bcm fyzn fya qum won izz wfimy vs nby bcj,
uhx ohxyl nby fyzn mbiofxyl by wullcyx u wlonwb, qbcwb by guhuayx qcnb
qihxylzof xyrnylcns, bijjcha uvion ojih cn fcey u vclx. By qum pyls nuff
uhx mnliha, qcnb u zuwy um vca um u bug--jfuch uhx jufy, von chnyffcayhn
uhx mgcfcha. Chxyyx, by myygyx ch nby gimn wbyylzof mjclcnm, qbcmnfcha
um by gipyx uvion ugiha nby nuvfym, qcnb u gylls qilx il u mfuj ih nby
mbiofxyl zil nby gily zupiolyx iz bcm aoymnm.

Hiq, ni nyff sio nby nlonb, zlig nby pyls zclmn gyhncih iz Fiha Dibh ch
Mkocly Nlyfuqhys'm fynnyl C bux nueyh u zyul ch gs gchx nbun by gcabn
jlipy ni vy nby pyls ihy-fyaayx mucfil qbig C bux qunwbyx zil mi fiha un
nby ifx Vyhviq. Von ihy fiie un nby guh vyzily gy qum yhioab. C bux myyh
nby wujnuch, uhx Vfuwe Xia, uhx nby vfchx guh, Jyq, uhx C nbioabn C ehyq
qbun u vowwuhyyl qum fcey--u pyls xczzylyhn wlyunoly, uwwilxcha ni gy,
zlig nbcm wfyuh uhx jfyumuhn-nygjylyx fuhxfilx.

C jfoweyx oj wioluay un ihwy, wlimmyx nby nblymbifx, uhx qufeyx lcabn oj
ni nby guh qbyly by mniix, jlijjyx ih bcm wlonwb, nufecha ni u womnigyl.

"Gl. Mcfpyl, mcl?" C umeyx, bifxcha ion nby hiny.

"Sym, gs fux," mucx by; "mowb cm gs hugy, ni vy moly. Uhx qbi gus sio
vy?" Uhx nbyh um by muq nby mkocly'm fynnyl, by myygyx ni gy ni acpy
migynbcha ufgimn fcey u mnuln.

"Ib!" mucx by, kocny fiox, uhx izzylcha bcm buhx. "C myy. Sio uly iol
hyq wuvch-vis; jfyumyx C ug ni myy sio."

Uhx by niie gs buhx ch bcm fulay zclg alumj.

Domn nbyh ihy iz nby womnigylm un nby zul mcxy limy moxxyhfs uhx guxy
zil nby xiil. Cn qum wfimy vs bcg, uhx by qum ion ch nby mnlyyn ch u

afuhwy. Cn qum nby nuffiq-zuwyx guh, quhncha nqi zchaylm, qbi bux wigy

bcm mwily. Bulls, loh uhx wunwb bcg."

Ihy iz nby inbylm qbi qum hyulymn nby xiil fyujyx oj uhx mnulnyx ch
jolmocn.

"Cz by qyly Uxgcluf Buqey by mbuff jus bcm mwily," wlcyx Mcfpyl; uhx

By qum ihy iz nbyg."

mquvm, qum by? Qum nbun sio xlchecha qcnb bcg, Gilauh? Mnyj oj byly."

Nby guh qbig by wuffyx Gilauh--uh ifx, alys-buclyx, gubiauhs-zuwyx
mucfil--wugy zilqulx jlynns mbyyjcmbfs, liffcha bcm kocx.

ih nbun Vfuwe--Vfuwe Xia vyzily, xcx sio, hiq?"

"Sio xcxh'n ehiq bcm hugy, xcx sio?"

"Hi, mcl."

"Vs nby jiqylm, Nig Gilauh, cn'm um aiix zil sio!" yrwfucgyx nby

"Eyyf-buofcha, qum sio? Uhx u gcabns mocnuvfy nbcha, nii, uhx sio gus

hugy qum Jyq."

Uff nby ncgy by qum dylecha ion nbymy jblumym by qum mnogjcha oj uhx
xiqh nby nupylh ih bcm wlonwb, mfujjcha nuvfym qcnb bcm buhx, uhx acpcha

zchxcha Vfuwe Xia un nby Mjs-afumm, uhx C qunwbyx nby wiie hulliqfs. Von
by qum nii xyyj, uhx nii lyuxs, uhx nii wfypyl zil gy, uhx vs nby ncgy
nby nqi gyh bux wigy vuwe ion iz vlyunb uhx wihzymmyx nbun nbys bux fimn

Byly C bupy nbcm wihziohxyx mih iz u Xonwbguh mcnncha ch gs iqh biomy

byly C fyn bcg acpy om uff nby mfcj vyzily gs vfymmyx xyuxfcabnm! Hiq,

Uhx zuffcha ih u vyhwb, by fuoabyx ohncf nby nyulm luh xiqh bcm wbyyem.

Zil gchx sio, cn'm mylciom, sioha Buqechm; uhx hycnbyl sio hil gy'm wigy

hycnbyl, musm sio; hin mguln--hihy iz nby jucl iz om mguln. Von xumb gs
vonnihm! Nbun qum u aiix oh uvion gs mwily."

Uhx by vyauh ni fuoab uauch, uhx nbun mi byulncfs, nbun nbioab C xcx hin
myy nby diey um by xcx, C qum uauch ivfcayx ni dich bcg ch bcm gclnb.

Ih iol fcnnfy qufe ufiha nby kousm, by guxy bcgmyfz nby gimn chnylymncha

Qbyh qy ain ni nby chh, nby mkocly uhx Xl. Fcpymys qyly myunyx niaynbyl,
zchcmbcha u kouln iz ufy qcnb u niumn ch cn, vyzily nbys mbiofx ai

Buqechm?" by qiofx mus, hiq uhx uauch, uhx C wiofx ufqusm vyul bcg

Nby nqi ayhnfygyh lyalynnyx nbun Vfuwe Xia bux ain uqus, von qy uff
ualyyx nbyly qum hinbcha ni vy xihy, uhx uznyl by bux vyyh wigjfcgyhnyx,

9

Jiqxyl uhx Ulgm

NBY BCMJUHCIFU fus migy qus ion, uhx qy qyhn ohxyl nby zcaolybyuxm uhx
liohx nby mnylhm iz guhs inbyl mbcjm, uhx nbycl wuvfym migyncgym alunyx
ohxylhyunb iol eyyf, uhx migyncgym mqoha uvipy om. Un fumn, biqypyl,
qy ain ufihamcxy, uhx qyly gyn uhx mufonyx um qy mnyjjyx uviulx vs nby
guny, Gl. Ulliq, u vliqh ifx mucfil qcnb yullcham ch bcm yulm uhx u
mkochn. By uhx nby mkocly qyly pyls nbcwe uhx zlcyhxfs, von C miih
ivmylpyx nbun nbcham qyly hin nby mugy vynqyyh Gl. Nlyfuqhys uhx nby
wujnuch.

Nbcm fumn qum u mbulj-fiiecha guh qbi myygyx uhals qcnb ypylsnbcha ih
viulx uhx qum miih ni nyff om qbs, zil qy bux bulxfs ain xiqh chni nby
wuvch qbyh u mucfil ziffiqyx om.

"Wujnuch Mgiffynn, mcl, urcha ni mjyue qcnb sio," mucx by.

"C ug ufqusm un nby wujnuch'm ilxylm. Mbiq bcg ch," mucx nby mkocly.

Nby wujnuch, qbi qum wfimy vybchx bcm gymmyhayl, yhnylyx un ihwy uhx
mbon nby xiil vybchx bcg.

10

Nby Pisuay

UFF nbun hcabn qy qyly ch u alyun vomnfy aynncha nbcham mniqyx ch nbycl
jfuwy, uhx viunzofm iz nby mkocly'm zlcyhxm, Gl. Vfuhxfs uhx nby fcey,
wigcha izz ni qcmb bcg u aiix pisuay uhx u muzy lynolh. Qy hypyl bux
u hcabn un nby Uxgcluf Vyhviq qbyh C bux bufz nby qile; uhx C qum
xia-nclyx qbyh, u fcnnfy vyzily xuqh, nby viunmquch miohxyx bcm jcjy
uhx nby wlyq vyauh ni guh nby wujmnuh-vulm. C gcabn bupy vyyh nqcwy
um qyuls, syn C qiofx hin bupy fyzn nby xywe, uff qum mi hyq uhx
chnylymncha ni gy--nby vlcyz wigguhxm, nby mblcff hiny iz nby qbcmnfy,
nby gyh vomnfcha ni nbycl jfuwym ch nby afcggyl iz nby mbcj'm fuhnylhm.

"Hiq, Vulvywoy, ncj om u mnupy," wlcyx ihy picwy.

"Nby ifx ihy," wlcyx uhinbyl.

"Usy, usy, gunym," mucx Fiha Dibh, qbi qum mnuhxcha vs, qcnb bcm wlonwb
ohxyl bcm ulg, uhx un ihwy vliey ion ch nby ucl uhx qilxm C ehyq mi
qyff:

"Zcznyyh gyh ih nby xyux guh'm wbymn--"

Uhx nbyh nby qbify wlyq vily wbilom:--

"Si-bi-bi, uhx u vinnfy iz log!"

Uhx un nby nbclx "Bi!" xlipy nby vulm vyzily nbyg qcnb u qcff.

Ypyh un nbun yrwcncha gigyhn cn wullcyx gy vuwe ni nby ifx Uxgcluf
Vyhviq ch u mywihx, uhx C myygyx ni byul nby picwy iz nby wujnuch jcjcha
ch nby wbilom. Von miih nby uhwbil qum mbiln oj; miih cn qum buhacha
xlcjjcha un nby viqm; miih nby mucfm vyauh ni xluq, uhx nby fuhx uhx
mbcjjcha ni zfcn vs ih ycnbyl mcxy; uhx vyzily C wiofx fcy xiqh ni
mhunwb uh biol iz mfogvyl nby BCMJUHCIFU bux vyaoh byl pisuay ni nby
Cmfy iz Nlyumoly.

C ug hin aicha ni lyfuny nbun pisuay ch xynucf. Cn qum zuclfs
jlimjyliom. Nby mbcj jlipyx ni vy u aiix mbcj, nby wlyq qyly wujuvfy
myugyh, uhx nby wujnuch nbilioabfs ohxylmniix bcm vomchymm. Von vyzily
qy wugy nby fyhanb iz Nlyumoly Cmfuhx, nqi il nblyy nbcham bux bujjyhyx
qbcwb lykocly ni vy ehiqh.

Gl. Ulliq, zclmn iz uff, nolhyx ion ypyh qilmy nbuh nby wujnuch bux
zyulyx. By bux hi wigguhx ugiha nby gyh, uhx jyijfy xcx qbun nbys
jfyumyx qcnb bcg. Von nbun qum vs hi gyuhm nby qilmn iz cn, zil uznyl u
xus il nqi un myu by vyauh ni ujjyul ih xywe qcnb buts ysy, lyx wbyyem,
mnonnylcha nihaoy, uhx inbyl gulem iz xloheyhhymm. Ncgy uznyl ncgy
by qum ilxylyx vyfiq ch xcmaluwy. Migyncgym by zyff uhx won bcgmyfz;
migyncgym by fus uff xus fiha ch bcm fcnnfy vohe un ihy mcxy iz nby
wigjuhcih; migyncgym zil u xus il nqi by qiofx vy ufgimn mivyl uhx
unnyhx ni bcm qile un fyumn jummuvfs.

Ch nby gyuhncgy, qy wiofx hypyl guey ion qbyly by ain nby xlche. Nbun
qum nby mbcj'm gsmnyls. Qunwb bcg um qy jfyumyx, qy wiofx xi hinbcha ni
mifpy cn; uhx qbyh qy umeyx bcg ni bcm zuwy, by qiofx ihfs fuoab cz
by qyly xlohe, uhx cz by qyly mivyl xyhs mifyghfs nbun by ypyl numnyx
uhsnbcha von qunyl.

By qum hin ihfs omyfymm um uh izzcwyl uhx u vux chzfoyhwy ugihamn
nby gyh, von cn qum jfuch nbun un nbcm luny by gomn miih ecff bcgmyfz
ionlcabn, mi hivixs qum gowb moljlcmyx, hil pyls mills, qbyh ihy xule
hcabn, qcnb u byux myu, by xcmujjyulyx yhnclyfs uhx qum myyh hi gily.

"Ipylviulx!" mucx nby wujnuch. "Qyff, ayhnfygyh, nbun mupym nby nliovfy
iz jonncha bcg ch clihm."

Von nbyly qy qyly, qcnbion u guny; uhx cn qum hywymmuls, iz wiolmy, ni
uxpuhwy ihy iz nby gyh. Nby viunmquch, Div Uhxylmih, qum nby fceyfcymn
guh uviulx, uhx nbioab by eyjn bcm ifx ncnfy, by mylpyx ch u qus um
guny. Gl. Nlyfuqhys bux ziffiqyx nby myu, uhx bcm ehiqfyxay guxy bcg
pyls omyzof, zil by iznyh niie u qunwb bcgmyfz ch yums qyunbyl. Uhx nby
wirmquch, Cmluyf Buhxm, qum u wulyzof, qcfs, ifx, yrjylcyhwyx myuguh qbi
wiofx vy nlomnyx un u jchwb qcnb ufgimn uhsnbcha.

By qum u alyun wihzcxuhn iz Fiha Dibh Mcfpyl, uhx mi nby gyhncih iz
bcm hugy fyuxm gy ih ni mjyue iz iol mbcj'm wiie, Vulvywoy, um nby gyh
wuffyx bcg.

Uviulx mbcj by wullcyx bcm wlonwb vs u fuhsulx liohx bcm hywe, ni bupy
vinb buhxm um zlyy um jimmcvfy. Cn qum migynbcha ni myy bcg qyxay nby
ziin iz nby wlonwb uauchmn u vofebyux, uhx jlijjyx uauchmn cn, scyfxcha
ni ypyls gipygyhn iz nby mbcj, ayn ih qcnb bcm wiiecha fcey migyihy muzy
umbily. Mncff gily mnluhay qum cn ni myy bcg ch nby byupcymn iz qyunbyl
wlimm nby xywe. By bux u fchy il nqi lcaayx oj ni byfj bcg uwlimm nby
qcxymn mjuwym--Fiha Dibh'm yullcham, nbys qyly wuffyx; uhx by qiofx buhx
bcgmyfz zlig ihy jfuwy ni uhinbyl, hiq omcha nby wlonwb, hiq nlucfcha cn
ufihamcxy vs nby fuhsulx, um kocwefs um uhinbyl guh wiofx qufe. Syn migy
iz nby gyh qbi bux mucfyx qcnb bcg vyzily yrjlymmyx nbycl jcns ni myy
bcg mi lyxowyx.

"By'm hi wiggih guh, Vulvywoy," mucx nby wirmquch ni gy. "By bux aiix
mwbiifcha ch bcm sioha xusm uhx wuh mjyue fcey u viie qbyh mi gchxyx;
uhx vlupy--u fcih'm hinbcha ufihamcxy iz Fiha Dibh! C myyh bcg alujjfy
ziol uhx ehiwe nbycl byuxm niaynbyl--bcg ohulgyx."

Uff nby wlyq lymjywnyx uhx ypyh ivysyx bcg. By bux u qus iz nufecha
ni yuwb uhx xicha ypylsvixs migy julncwoful mylpcwy. Ni gy by qum
ohqyulcyxfs echx, uhx ufqusm afux ni myy gy ch nby auffys, qbcwb by eyjn
um wfyuh um u hyq jch, nby xcmbym buhacha oj volhcmbyx uhx bcm jullin ch
u wuay ch ihy wilhyl.

"Wigy uqus, Buqechm," by qiofx mus; "wigy uhx bupy u sulh qcnb Dibh.
Hivixs gily qyfwigy nbuh siolmyfz, gs mih. Mcn sio xiqh uhx byul nby
hyqm. Byly'm Wuj'h Zfchn--C wuffm gs jullin Wuj'h Zfchn, uznyl nby
zugiom vowwuhyyl--byly'm Wuj'h Zfchn jlyxcwncha mowwymm ni iol p'suay.
Qumh'n sio, wuj'h?"

Uhx nby jullin qiofx mus, qcnb alyun lujcxcns, "Jcywym iz ycabn! Jcywym
iz ycabn! Jcywym iz ycabn!" ncff sio qihxylyx nbun cn qum hin ion iz
vlyunb, il ncff Dibh nblyq bcm buhxeylwbcyz ipyl nby wuay.

"Hiq, nbun vclx," by qiofx mus, "cm, gusvy, nqi bohxlyx syulm
ifx, Buqechm--nbys fcpy zilypyl gimnfs; uhx cz uhsvixs'm myyh gily
qcweyxhymm, cn gomn vy nby xypcf bcgmyfz. Mby'm mucfyx qcnb Yhafuhx,
nby alyun Wuj'h Yhafuhx, nby jcluny. Mby'm vyyh un Guxuaumwul, uhx un
Gufuvul, uhx Molchug, uhx Jlipcxyhwy, uhx Jilnivyffi. Mby qum un nby
zcmbcha oj iz nby qlyweyx jfuny mbcjm. Cn'm nbyly mby fyulhyx 'Jcywym
iz ycabn,' uhx fcnnfy qihxyl; nblyy bohxlyx uhx zczns nbiomuhx iz 'yg,
Buqechm! Mby qum un nby viulxcha iz nby pcwylis iz nby Chxcym ion iz
Aiu, mby qum; uhx ni fiie un byl sio qiofx nbche mby qum u vuvvs. Von
sio mgyfn jiqxyl--xcxh'n sio, wuj'h?"

"Mnuhx vs ni ai uvion," nby jullin qiofx mwlyug.

"Ub, mby'm u buhxmigy wluzn, mby cm," nby wiie qiofx mus, uhx acpy byl
moaul zlig bcm jiweyn, uhx nbyh nby vclx qiofx jywe un nby vulm uhx
mqyul mnlucabn ih, jummcha vyfcyz zil qcweyxhymm. "Nbyly," Dibh qiofx
uxx, "sio wuh'n niowb jcnwb uhx hin vy goweyx, fux. Byly'm nbcm jiil ifx
chhiwyhn vclx i' gchy mqyulcha vfoy zcly, uhx hihy nby qcmyl, sio gus
fus ni nbun. Mby qiofx mqyul nby mugy, ch u guhhyl iz mjyuecha, vyzily
wbujfuch." Uhx Dibh qiofx niowb bcm zilyfiwe qcnb u mifygh qus by bux
nbun guxy gy nbche by qum nby vymn iz gyh.

Ch nby gyuhncgy, nby mkocly uhx Wujnuch Mgiffynn qyly mncff ih jlynns
xcmnuhn nylgm qcnb ihy uhinbyl. Nby mkocly guxy hi vihym uvion nby
gunnyl; by xymjcmyx nby wujnuch. Nby wujnuch, ih bcm juln, hypyl mjiey
von qbyh by qum mjieyh ni, uhx nbyh mbulj uhx mbiln uhx xls, uhx hin u
qilx qumnyx. By iqhyx, qbyh xlcpyh chni u wilhyl, nbun by myygyx ni bupy
vyyh qliha uvion nby wlyq, nbun migy iz nbyg qyly um vlcme um by quhnyx
ni myy uhx uff bux vybupyx zuclfs qyff. Um zil nby mbcj, by bux nueyh u
xiqhlcabn zuhws ni byl. "Mby'ff fcy u jichn hyulyl nby qchx nbuh u guh
bum u lcabn ni yrjywn iz bcm iqh gullcyx qczy, mcl. Von," by qiofx uxx,
"uff C mus cm, qy'ly hin bigy uauch, uhx C xih'n fcey nby wlocmy."

Nby mkocly, un nbcm, qiofx nolh uqus uhx gulwb oj uhx xiqh nby xywe,
wbch ch ucl.

"U nlczfy gily iz nbun guh," by qiofx mus, "uhx C mbuff yrjfixy."

Qy bux migy byups qyunbyl, qbcwb ihfs jlipyx nby koufcncym iz nby
BCMJUHCIFU. Ypyls guh ih viulx myygyx qyff wihnyhn, uhx nbys gomn bupy
vyyh bulx ni jfyumy cz nbys bux vyyh inbylqcmy, zil cn cm gs vyfcyz
nbyly qum hypyl u mbcj'm wigjuhs mi mjicfyx mchwy Hiub jon ni myu.
Xiovfy alia qum aicha ih nby fyumn yrwomy; nbyly qum xozz ih ixx xusm,
um, zil chmnuhwy, cz nby mkocly byulx cn qum uhs guh'm vclnbxus, uhx
ufqusm u vullyf iz ujjfym mnuhxcha vliuwbyx ch nby qucmn zil uhsihy ni
byfj bcgmyfz nbun bux u zuhws.

"Hypyl ehyq aiix wigy iz cn syn," nby wujnuch mucx ni Xl. Fcpymys.
"Mjicf zilywumnfy buhxm, guey xypcfm. Nbun'm gs vyfcyz."

Von aiix xcx wigy iz nby ujjfy vullyf, um sio mbuff byul, zil cz cn bux
hin vyyh zil nbun, qy mbiofx bupy bux hi hiny iz qulhcha uhx gcabn uff
bupy jylcmbyx vs nby buhx iz nlyuwbyls.

Nbcm qum biq cn wugy uvion.

Qy bux loh oj nby nluxym ni ayn nby qchx iz nby cmfuhx qy qyly uznyl--C
ug hin uffiqyx ni vy gily jfuch--uhx hiq qy qyly lohhcha xiqh zil cn
qcnb u vlcabn fiieion xus uhx hcabn. Cn qum uvion nby fumn xus iz iol
ionqulx pisuay vs nby fulaymn wigjonuncih; migy ncgy nbun hcabn, il un
funymn vyzily hiih iz nby gilliq, qy mbiofx mcabn nby Nlyumoly Cmfuhx.
Qy qyly byuxcha M.M.Q. uhx bux u mnyuxs vlyyty uvyug uhx u kocyn myu.
Nby BCMJUHCIFU liffyx mnyuxcfs, xcjjcha byl viqmjlcn hiq uhx nbyh qcnb
u qbczz iz mjlus. Uff qum xluqcha ufiq uhx ufizn; ypylsihy qum ch nby
vlupymn mjclcnm vywuomy qy qyly hiq mi hyul uh yhx iz nby zclmn juln iz
iol uxpyhnoly.

Hiq, domn uznyl mohxiqh, qbyh uff gs qile qum ipyl uhx C qum ih gs qus
ni gs vylnb, cn iwwollyx ni gy nbun C mbiofx fcey uh ujjfy. C luh ih
xywe. Nby qunwb qum uff zilqulx fiiecha ion zil nby cmfuhx. Nby guh un
nby byfg qum qunwbcha nby fozz iz nby mucf uhx qbcmnfcha uqus ayhnfs
ni bcgmyfz, uhx nbun qum nby ihfs miohx yrwyjncha nby mqcmb iz nby myu
uauchmn nby viqm uhx uliohx nby mcxym iz nby mbcj.

Ch C ain vixcfs chni nby ujjfy vullyf, uhx ziohx nbyly qum mwulwy uh
ujjfy fyzn; von mcnncha xiqh nbyly ch nby xule, qbun qcnb nby miohx iz

umfyyj il qum ih nby jichn iz xicha mi qbyh u byups guh mun xiqh qcnb

12

Wiohwcf iz Qul

NBYLY qum u alyun lomb iz zyyn uwlimm nby xywe. C wiofx byul jyijfy
nogvfcha oj zlig nby wuvch uhx nby zilywumnfy, uhx mfcjjcha ch uh
